so'hamiti | ayaṃ pramātā kālādipañcaka veṣṭitobhāti | eṣāṃ   
kālādīnāmanyatrarakto'pi niyatyānyat kāryata iti eṣāṃ kālādīnāṃ   
bhinnaviṣayatvamapi bhavati | anenāsya dehādeḥ svātantryāt   
parameśvarasyaiva svātantryaṃ ca darśitam | ete ca kālādaya   
uktakrameṇedānīntano'haṃ kiñcijjñohaṃ (ṭp. 359) kiñcit kartāhaṃ   
atrarakto'haṃ tatrāpyatraiva rakto'hamityuktakrameṇapramātṛlagnataiva   
bhātīti tasya māyā pramātṛśaktisvarūpastadvyabhicāriṇaḥ   
pramātṛbhinnā eva ete sarvapramātṝṇāmekaprakārā na bhavati prati   
pramātṛbhinnā eva ete sarvapramātṝṇāmeka prakārā na bhavati |   
pratipramātṛbhinnā api naṭamallaprekṣādau kālādayaḥ   
sarvapramātṝṇāmekī bhaveyuḥ | kalādīnāmīśvarecchā vyatiriktaṃ   
sahajajīvitaṃ nāstīti svāminaścātmsaṃsthasyetyādau asakṛduktam | eṣa   
pramātā māyāndha ityatra vakṣyate ca -  
  
	svavyatirikte meye mātā pramāteti pūrvaśloke yaduktaṃ tatrokte tat   
prameyaṃ pramātṛ vyatiriktaṃ prameyaṃ darśayati |  
  
	trayoviṃśatiprakāraṃ pṛthivyādi śabdānta   
sthūlasūkṣmātmakaṃ kāryarūpaṃ (462) bahirindriyātmakaṃ   
karaṇarūpaṃ prameyaṃ yat tasya kāryakāraṇarūpasya   
kāryakāraṇairavibhaktaṃ svayamekaṃ eṣāṃ mūlakāraṇaṃ pradhānaṃ   
ca yat tatsarvaṃ meyam |  
  
	kāryakāraṇarūpaṃ trayoviṃśati prakāraṃ yat sarvakāryasya   
kāraṇasya ca sukhaduḥkhamohamayatvāt tairavibhāgarūpaṃ prakṛtitatvaṃ   
yat tatsarvaṃ meyamiti saṃbandhaḥ | māyottīrṇānāṃ yogināṃ   
mantrapramātṝṇāṃ tadīśvarātmamatreśvarāṇāṃ   
mantramaheśvarāṇāṃ ca mātṝṇāṃ pṛthivyādibhūtapañcakasya   
gandhādi tanmātrā pañcakasyopasthādi vāgāntasya karmendriya   
pañcakasya ghrāṇādi śrotrāntajñānendriyapañcakasya mana ādi   
buddhyantāntaḥkaraṇatrayasyāsya sarvasya viṣayīkāreṇa   
vaśīkaraṇayogitvāt sarvameva prameyaṃ māyāpramātṝṇāmapi   
pratyakṣatvā bhāve'pi anumānadiśā āgamadiśā ca pṛthivyādi   
prameyamevetī yat prameyaṃ pṛthivyādi prakṛtyantatatvaṃ prameyaṃ   
pūrvaślokoktāḥ kālavidyā kālārāganiyatayastu api   
tatvāntargatatvānmāyāpramātṛ vyatiriktaprameyanirūpaṇād   
asminnavasare kālādayaḥ prameyā api na prameyatvena gaṇitāḥ vastutaḥ   
atratyaḥ māyādikṣityanta tatva madhyavartī pramātā prameya eva | sa tu   
māyā pramātā prameya bhūto'pi svavyatiriktaṃ prameyaṃ   
pratiparameśvarasya māyātmikāyāḥ svātantryaśaktyā pramātrī   
kriyamāṇa prameyatve satyapyācchādita prameyatāka ihocyate | atra   
pṛthivyādi buddhyantatatvatrayoviṃśati madhye kiṃ (ṭp. 360) kāryaṃ kiṃ   
ca kāraṇamityante vā si praśnamāśaṅkyāha | atra trayoviṃśatau   
bāhyakaraṇāvalī antaḥ (463) karaṇāvalī trayodaśavidyā   
sthūlasūkṣmatvabhedataḥ kāryavargaśca daśadhā māyā pramātuḥ   
prathamaṃ karaṇarūpayogaprayojanamiti ādau karaṇānāṃ kathanam |   
tāni trayodaśa | tatra karaṇe ṣvavarohakrameṇādau pṛthivyādi   
śabdāntādhyavasāya sāmānyamātrarūpā buddhiḥ adhyavasāya   
sādhanaṃ buddhiriti muktanītyā svayaṃ pramātṛviṣayādhyavasāya   
sādhanarūpatvādyādyasmin yasmin viṣaye pramāturyoyo'dhyavasāyo'sti   
tat tadadhyavasāya sāmānyamātrarūpā trayoviṃśattatvātmikā buddhiḥ   
| anena buddhervyāpakātmakā tatvatā darśitā | ahaṃkāro mamedaṃ na   
mamedamityabhimānasādhanamityukta nītyābhimānasādhanatvāt yasya   
yasya pramātuḥ yatra yatra grāhye viṣaye ahaṃ grāhakaḥ mamedaṃ   
pṛthivyādi grāhyaṃ na mamedammiti māyīyo yo'bhimāno'sti tat   
tadabhimāna sāmānyamātrarūpo'haṃkāraḥ manaḥ   
saṅkalpavikalpasādhanamityuktanītyā pṛthivyādiśabdāntaṃ saṅkalpaṃ   
sarveṣu kāryeṣu evaṃ karomi evaṃ na karomīti sarvakāryakartranusthūta   
sāmānyātmakasaṃkalpakāraṇaṃ manaḥ ityetattrayaṃ pramātuḥ   
antaḥkaraṇaṃ pṛthivyādi śabdāntaṃ sthūlasūkṣmaṃ viṣayamantaḥ   
karomītyantaḥkaraṇaṃ śabdādi pṛthivyantavastvadhyavasāyarūpāyāṃ   
jñānātmani buddhau upayogonīndriyāṇi jñānendriyāṇi   
pañcaśabdādhyavasāyarūpe jñāne upayogi śrotrendriyaṃ   
sparśādhyavasāyarūpe jñāne upayogisparśendriyamityādi yatra yatra   
śabdādhyavasāya jñānamasti tatra tatra śrotramupayogīti śrotrendriyasya   
vyāpakātmakaṃ tatvamityādi krameṇa sarveṣāmindiryāṇāṃ   
vyāpakarūpaṃ tattvamavagantavyam | yathoktam -   
śabdasparśarūparasagandhātmanāṃ viṣayāṇāṃ krameṇa   
grahaṇasādhanāni (464) śrotratvak   
cakṣurjihvāghrāṇānipañcajñānendriyāṇi vacanādāna   
gamanavisargānandātmani karmāṇyupayogīni pāṭavādighrāṇāntānti |   
karmāṇyupayogitvameva karmendriyāṇāṃ pratipādayati - tathā   
hītyādinā | tyāgaṃ grahaṇaṃ, tyāgagrahaṇayordvayamiti   
bahirindriyaviṣayaṃ yat karma teṣu tyāge grahaṇe ubhaye ca krameṇa   
pāyuḥ pāṇiḥ pāda iti karaṇāni vyāpriyante | pādendriyasyaikasya   
deśatyāgaḥ ityubhayamapyasti | etat tyāgahaṇadvayamantaḥ   
prāṇapramātari yenendriyeṇa kriyate (ṭp. 361) (464) tadvagindriyaṃ   
mūlādhārāt prabhṛti jihvā paryantaprasāraṇātmani prasaramekamekaṃ   
sthānaṃ tyaktvā anyamanyaṃ sthānaṃ gṛhṇātīti tyāgagrahaṇātmakaṃ   
karmadvayamasti | tyāga grahaṇātmakavyāpārakṣobhapraśāntyā   
ānandātmakaviśrānti kriyopayogyupasyendriyaṃ jñānendriyavargāt   
karmendriya vargasya viśeṣaḥ tāmasāhaṅkāraviśeṣātmakāni   
karmendriyāṇi sarvadehavyāpakāni vyapakatvācchinnāgrahastaḥ   
bāhubhyāmādadānaḥ haste naivādatte | cchinnapādaḥ jānubhyāmeva   
gacchati | kevalamasphuṭapūrṇādānādi vyavahāralābhasthānatvāt   
pañcāṅgulīrūpamadhiṣṭhānamucyate | ityevaṃ buddhyādyupasthāntāni   
karaṇāni trayodaśa śrotrādīnikaraṇāni gotva ghaṭatvādivat   
śivādisakalāntapramātṛ gata śrotrādiṣvanusyūtatvāt sāmānyarūpāṇi   
tatvānyeva | eṣāṃ śrotrādīnāṃ paramapramātāraṃ   
pratikāryatvepyasādhāraṇe na kāryatvena vyapadeśaḥ eteṣāmeva   
kāraṇatvena vyapadeśaḥ, natvanyasya kartṛvargasya kāryavargasya ca   
kāraṇatvam | atrārohakrame gandhādiṃ vihāya pṛthivyāderūpādānaṃ   
gandhādivargasya pṛthivyādyantarbhūtatvāt sthūlāni kāryāṇi   
pṛthivyādīni pañcaiṣāṃ pṛthivyādīnāṃ sūkṣmaṃ rūpaṃ krameṇa   
gandho raso rūpasparśaśabda iti | (465) śabdaikagaṇamākāśam |   
śabdaikaguṇavyāpitvādākāśaṃ tvamambike |  
  
	śabdasparśātmakaṃ tattvaṃ tadguṇaṃ vyūhakṛt pare ||  
	  
	vāyuḥ prāṇādirūpeṇa sthitastvatprakṛtirmataḥ |  
	yaḥ śabdasparśarūpāṇāṃ saṃsthānaṃ tadguṇasya yat ||  
  
	tejo vikārastvadrūpa pare pākādi kāryakṛt ||  
	yaḥ śive śabdasaṃsparśarūpaiḥ sākaṃ rasātmanā ||  
  
	tanmātreṇodbhavantyāpastāstvatsaṃgrahayonayaḥ |  
	śabdādibhiścaturbhiryā gandhena ca vibhāvyate ||  
  
	tatkāryā ca bhavet pṛthvī pṛthvī sā tvaṃ nigadyase ||  
  
ityekaikaguṇaiveti | iha tatvamātragaṇanāyāmanupayogāt   
pṛthivyaptejovāyurnabha iti vibhaktaṃ pṛthivyādisthūlaṃ   
gandhādyavibhāgasyānumāpakaṃ jñāpakaṃ prathamaṃ   
sthūlapañcakaṃ darśitam | tatra tattvagaṇanāyāṃ pṛthivyādayaḥ   
śabdāntāḥ (ṭp. 362) miśrī | bhūya ghaṭapaṭādi svalakṣaṇībhūtāḥ   
vāgādibhiḥ karmendriyaiḥ prasarpitāḥ gṛhītāḥ   
śrotrādijñānendriyairālocitāḥ manasā saṃkalpitāḥ ahaṅkāreṇa   
mamedamityābhimatā buddhyāniścitāḥ aśuddhavidyayā vivecitāḥ   
kalādibhiścaturbhirabhirañjitāḥ pṛthivyādyābhāsaḥ ityevaṃ krameṇa   
pramātariviśrāmyatīti tātparyam | sarvāṇi tatvāni pramātari   
viśrāmyantītyarthaḥ | etacca tat pradhāneṣu tattvagaṇanā pradhāneṣu   
tattattattva tattatpramātṛnirūpaṇapradhāneṣu śrītantrālokatrikasārādiṣu   
nirṇītamiti iha tattvamātragaṇanāyāmanupayogaṃ na vistāritam ||  
  
(466) iti śrīpratyabhijñāsūtravimarśinī vyākhyāyāṃ   
trayodaśamāhnikam ||  
  
  
  
atha caturdaśamāhnikam   
  
	āgamādhikāre prathamāhnikena śivādikṣityantatattvātmaka   
prameya nirūpaṇaṃ kṛtam | anena dvitīyenāhnikena māyādikṣityanta   
pramātrādiśivādi pramātṛsaptakanirūpaṇaṃ tatpramātṛtānyonya   
tāratamyapratipādanātmakamāṇavādi malatrayanirūpaṇaṃ tanmeya   
trayanirūpaṇaṃ tanmalatrayodbhavatirobhāvabhedāt saṃsāriṇāṃ   
bandhamokṣanirūpaṇaṃ prāṇāpāna vyānodāna samānātmaka   
jāgratsvapna suṣuptaturya turyātītāvasthā pañcakanirūpaṇaṃ ca kriyate |  
  
	akhaṇḍita iti | sarvajña sarvakartṛ satatodita sarvavyāpakatvātmaka   
cidānandaghanasvabhāva khaṇḍane'pi sakala pralayākala vijñānākala   
mantramantreśvaramantramaheśvarātmikāṃ vicitrāmanyonyaṃ bhinnāṃ   
mātṛkalpanāṃ suhṛnmaṇḍalacakre svasminnavināśini sahaje hṛnmaṇḍale   
sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhāranigrahānugrahātmaka kṛtyapañcakaparivartanakāritvāc   
cakrarūpe śrīparāśaktyātmanihṛdaye yaḥ prathayet paramārthataḥ   
svātmābhinnamapi darpaṇabiṃbagata nagaragrāmādivadanyonyataḥ   
svātmanaśca bhinnaṃ prakāśayet taṃ śivaṃ stumaḥ ||  
  
	evaṃ śivādikṣityanta tatvarāśau nirṇīte sati tattattatvāntarbhāve   
noktamapi (ṭp. 363) pramātṛtatvaṃ vitatya pradhānatayā pṛthageva   
nirgetuṃ kevalaṃ pramātṛ tatvameva vitatya tat pramātṛtatva svarūpaṃ   
vistareṇa pradarśya tatraitanmātṛtetyādibhiḥ (467) vyāno viśvātmakaḥ   
para ityantairviṃśatyā ślokairāhṇikaṃ prastūyate | asmin pratyabhijñā   
śāstrapramāturadhikāriṇaḥ sadgurukaṭākṣapavitri tasya svarūpa   
pratyabhijñānamupadiśyate | tathā hītyanena pramātṛtatvaheyopādeyatā   
vibhāganirūpaṇadvāreṇa tadubhayaṃ pramātṛtatvaṃ matsvarūpaṃ   
tasmādahamīśvara evetī śvarātmaka svarūpapratyabhijñānamasmin   
śāstra upadiśyate | sa upadeśyaḥ pramātā heyamupādeyañca   
śāstropadeśadvāreṇa heyamupādeyatvaṃ pramātṛtatvaṃ svaṃ   
svabhāvaṃ vidvān ubhayasyāpi svarūpatayā vedanaṃ   
paramopādeyarūpaṃ śivasya bhāvaṃ svātmānamabhedenāviśan   
jīvannevamukto bhavatīti śivalakṣaṇābhijñānabhūtaṃ   
jñānakriyāśaktiyuktatvāt śivasvabhāvaṃ svātmānaṃ yaḥ   
purāṇāgamādi prasiddha īśvaraḥ sa evāhamityabhedenāviśan   
jīvannevamukto bhavatīti ślokena māyā pramātṛvargasya saṃhārasṛṣṭi   
sthityavasthā trayādhikāri brahmaviṣṇurudrasvarūpanirūpaṇaṃ tato'pi   
dvayena heyopādeya pramātṛtattvaṃ māyāntarvartī pramātṛtatvoheyaḥ   
māyottīrṇapramātṛtatvavartī pramātṛvarga upādeya iti baddha(ndha)rūpa   
pramātṛvargoheyaḥ gurukaṭākṣānmukta upādeyaḥ | heyopādeyatvopayogi   
āṇavādimalasvarūpanirūpaṇaṃ malakṛtaṃ ca pramātṛbhedaṃ dvayena   
parameśvarātmaka svarūpasamāveśasvarūpaślokapañcakena   
suṣuptasvapna jāgratturīya turīyātītātmikāvasthā trayeṇa   
tāsāmavasthānaṃ heyopādeya nirūpaṇaṃ jāgradādi trayaṃ   
turyaturyatītātmakaṃ dvayamupādeyamiti nirūpayatyācāryaḥ tatreti |  
  
	evamāgamasiddhe yuktyanugate ca tatvasvarūpe nirūpite sati   
etanmātṛteti kālādikapañcakaveṣṭitopasaṃhṛta prameya jāta   
mātṛtāmātrasya (468) sthitau saṃhāradaśāyāṃ rudraḥ   
taddaśāsaṃpādanenopasaṃhṛta prameyadaśā saṃpādanena   
svopāsakalokasya taddaśādānena taddaśāddhyānāveśasampannasya   
svopāsakalokasya (ṭp. 364) svāmimukhyasaṃpādanena ca bhajamāno   
bhagavān rudro'dhidaivatam idamiti bhinnaprameya prasārātmani   
sṛṣṭyavasthāyāṃ brahmādidaivatatvena sthitaḥ prasṛte bhinnaprameye tat   
santānapravahaṇalakṣaṇaprasārātmani sthityavasthāyāṃ   
viṣṇuradhidaivatatvena sthitaḥ | tatra bhagavato rudrasyāhamiti   
pramātṛdaśāyuktatvāt prāṇāpānadina   
niśāsūryendvādidvandvavinirmuktatvāt   
brahmaviṣṇvostṛtīyanayanonmīlanatvaṃ nāsti |   
evamantarbahirvṛttirityādinā sthūlasūkṣmatvabhedata   
ityantenāgamakāṃḍa prathamāhnikena śivādikṣityante tatvavarge   
nirūpite sati kālādiveṣṭitaṃ māyāpramātṛtārūpaṃ yat tat pramātṛ   
rūpameva saṃhārākhyāyāṃ yasyāṃ prameyadaśāyāmupasaṃhṛte   
dantārūpaprameyajātam | ata eva pramātṛtā mātratvena sthitaṃ bhavati |   
tathāsvāṃ daśāyāṃ tasya pramāturadhiṣṭhātṛ devatā tvaṃ tasya   
pramātustad daśā saṃpādanena svopāsakalokasyopasaṃhṛtaprameya-  
jātamātṛtā mātrātmakasaṃhāradaśādānena ca |  
  
	kiñca tat saṃsāradaśādhyānasamāpannasyābhimukhya   
saṃpādanena cādhiṣṭhā tṛdevatā tvaṃ bhajamāna īśvara eva rudro   
bhagavān parameśvara eva bhagavān rudro bhūtvā sthitaḥ yo rudraḥ   
māyā pade'pi prāṇāpānamaya dharmādharma sūryendudinaniśādi   
dvandvavinirmuktāhaṃ tātmaka brahmanāḍīmayo dānātmaka   
vahnimayamadhye jyotīrūpaḥ (469) pramātṛsvarūpasparśādunmīlita   
tṛtīyanetrā madhyamajyotirbrahmanāḍī tasya māyā pramātuḥ svātmano   
bhinnasyedantārūpasya prameyasya prasare sṛṣṭyādi daśāyām   
adhiṣṭhātṛ devatā tvaṃ bhajana tasya pramāturā saṃhāraṃ   
prasṛtabhinnaprameya saṃtānapravahaṇalakṣaṇe prasare sthityavasthāyām   
adhiṣṭhātṛ devatā tvaṃ bhajanviṣṇustayorbrahmaviṣṇavorapi svorapi   
svopāsakalokasya taddaśāsṛṣṭisthiti daśādānaṃ tat sṛṣṭidaśā   
dhyānāveśasamānasya svopāsakalokasya svābhimukhya   
saṃpādanañcāsti | ata evedantā rūpaprameyasṛṣṭisthitīrūpasya meya   
saṃpādane prādhānyāt ata evāhamiti pramātṛ daśā veśa śūnyatvāt   
tayorna tṛtīyanayanonmīlanaṃ prasara iti pramātpatti sthityoḥ paryāyaḥ |  
  
	(ṭp. 365) pūrvasūtreṇa yat pramātṛsvarūpamuktaṃ tasya   
pramātṛsvarūpasya māyāṃ dhatve sati saṃsārī pramātā patiriti kathyate   
| tasyaiśvaryasya bhāvasyetyuktanītyā vidyābhijñāpitaiśvarye pramātari   
sati mukta iti vyapadeśaḥ | viśvasya svāṅgatvābhimānane   
ahamevāhamidamiti sadāśiveśvaradaśāyāṃ sampannāyāṃ tasya   
māyāpramātuḥ patirityāgamasiddhā saṃjñā | tirādhānakarī   
māyābhidhā punaḥ ityuktanītyā māyāśaktyā viśvasya svātmano   
bhedenābhimanane kleśakarmādi kaluṣaḥ paśurityāgamikā saṃjñā iti   
saṃsārīti muktaya iti patiriti paśuriti cāgamikāsaṃjñā bhedañca   
nirūpayati - eṣa iti | kālādi veṣṭitaḥ māyāndhaḥ ata eva   
karmabaṃdhanaḥ karmāṇi bandhakatvenābhimanyamānaḥ | eṣa iti   
kālādiveṣṭitaḥ śūnyādi pramātā saṃsārītyucyate | proktarūpa   
vidyābhijñāpitanityatvādyaiśvaryaḥ ata eva cidghanaḥ cidekarūpaḥ (470)   
mukta ityucyate | eva muktaṃ bhāveṣu svāṅgarūpeṣu pramātā kṣityādi   
bhāveṣu svāṅgatvena pramananaṃ kurvan patiriti kathyate | māyāvaśāt   
svātmano bhediṣu teṣu bhāveṣu pāśarūpaistaistairbhāvaiḥ pāśitatvāt |   
ata eva kleśakarmādi kaluṣa iti kathyate āgameṣu parameśvareṇeti śeṣaḥ |   
tirodhānakāriṇyā mayayā andhovimohitaḥ tiraskṛta svātmeśvarabhāvaḥ   
ata eva mohitaḥ kālādiveṣṭitaḥ śūnyādiḥ pramātā saṃsarati   
yoneryonyantaraṃ bhajatīti saṃsārī dehasyāpi saṃsaraṇamastītyāha -   
deho'pityādinā |  
  
	(471) na kevala va ------------ bu -----------------------------   
vanavārdhakeṣu tadbāhyādi svarūpasādṛśyamanuvartayan bālyādiṣu   
saṃsaratī va dehī | yathoktam -  
  
	dehino'sminyathā dehe kaumāraṃ yauvanaṃ jarā |  
	tathā dehāntaraprāptirdhārastatra na muhyati ||  
  
dehasyaikasminneva janmani bālyayauvanādiṣu saṃsaraṇam | anyonya   
rūpagrahaṇāt | buddhiprāṇādestu jantāntare'pi saṃsaraṇam | yathoktam -   
mano hi jātyantarasaṅgatijñamiti | api śabdena tattatkṣaṇika -----------------   
duḥkhamohāviṣṭatvāt ekasminnapi janmani saṃsaraṇamasti | tasyaiśvarya   
svabhāvasyetyuktanītyā maheśvarātmakasvasvarūpaprakāśanakāriṇyā   
vidyayā yasya pramāturaiśvaryaṃ pratyābhijñāpadaṃ prāpitaṃ (ṭp.   
365) pūrṇatvādyaiśvaryaṃ yasya pūrṇatvādyaiśvaryasya   
pratyabhijñāpanaprāṇanāt śarīrādyapi śarīraprāṇabuddhiśūnyāni   
tadvyatiriktaṃ ghaṭapaṭādi viśvamapi saṃvedanameva |   
ekasaṃvinmayamevābhimanyamānaḥ ata eva cidaikaghanā   
pūrṇāhantātmakabodhaikaghanā ata evānye dantātmakā   
cidrūpavyāmiśraṇā śūnyā cideva yasya svarūpaṃ saṃbhede sthite'pi   
dehapātānantaraṃ janmabandhavirahāt mukta iti vyapadeśayogyaḥ dehe   
patite tu yathā sthita śivaikarūpaḥ iti kaḥ pramātā saṃsaraṇahetu bhūtād   
dehādestasya pramātuśca śivaika ghanatvāt kaḥ kuto muktaḥ | yathoktam -   
namaḥ saṃsārarupāyeti | gurukaṭākṣapātāt pūrvapaśvavasthā rūpayā   
gatyā amukta caitramaitrādi pramātrantarāpekṣayā ca muktaḥ (472) śiva   
iti vyapadeśaṃ yo'yaṃ muktaḥ saḥ kṣityādi bhāvān saśarīratve   
nābhimanyamānaḥ kṣitirahamahaṃ pātho vaiśvānaro'hamahaṃ   
marudviyadahamiti nītyā kṣityādi bhāvān svaśarīratve   
nābhimandamānaḥ pramimīte pramananaṃ kareti mananamavagamanaṃ   
karoti | ata eva kṣityādibhāvānāṃ svāmī īśa īśvaraḥ   
patiśabdasyaiko'rthaḥ | ātmānamata evāyamityuktanītyā   
teṣāmaprakāśarūpasyātma paramārthasamarpaṇācca pālaka iti   
bhāvānāṃ patirupadiṣṭaḥ śāstre tattadrūpatayā svayameva   
prakāśanāt pālakorakṣakaḥ patirityupadiṣṭaḥ śāstre parameśvareṇa   
māyāto bhediṣu mātāsan māyāśaktyā svātmanaścānyonyaḥ   
kṛtabhedān | ata eva svātmano vyatiriktān yadābhimīte māyāśakti   
kṛtabhedaistaireva meyaiḥ pāśīta iti paśuraktaḥ | mamedaṃ kalatraṃ   
mamedaṃ kṣetraṃ mamāyaṃ putra ityādi baddhatvāt pāśita iti   
paśuruktaḥ ------------ ma -------------- raṇeti śeṣaḥ | tathā hi tyanena teṣāṃ   
meyānāṃ pāśatvamevadarśayati | ādyasya   
pramāturvedyarāśivaśādeva | vidyā svasvarūpā pratyabhijñām | asmitā   
tesvahaṅkāraḥ | rāgasteṣvabhiṣvaṃgaḥ dveṣastadviparītaḥ | abhiniveśa   
āveśa iti kleśāḥ saṃbhavanti | asya pramātuvedyarāśi vaśāt   
svarganarakaphalarūpāṇi karmāṇi bhavanti | ādiśabdenāśārūpā   
hṛdayasthā vāsanā teṣāṃ hṛdayasthitaḥ saṃskāraḥ kleśānāṃ   
phalātmaka bhogarūpo vipākaḥ ityavidyāsmitādirūpeṇa   
kāluṣyamanantaprakāraṃ kāluṣyaṃ māyāśaktyāvilatvaṃ yataḥ   
kāluṣyāt pāśitatvena paśuruktaḥ |  
  
	(ṭp. 367) (473) yadetaduktaṃ paśurūpaṃ tat paśurūpamevāṇa va   
māyīya karmātmakaṃ malamityāgameṣu parameśvareṇoktamityāha -   
citsvarūpatve satyapi pūrṇāhantātmaka svātaṃtryahāniḥ dehāhaṃ   
bhāvātmaka svātantryetyāpi bodhaśūnyatā ityāṇavaṃ malaṃ dvidhā |   
tatrahetuḥ jñātṛkartṛntātmakacittatva svarūpa hānito hetoḥ | tatra bodhasya   
svātaṃtrya hānirvijñānākāleṣu sakalapralayākaleṣu   
svātantryasyāpyabodhateti vibhāgaḥ | atraivaṃ dviprakāre āṇavamāyīye   
sthite sati bhinna vedyaprathā anyonya bhinnānāṃ svātmano bhinnānāṃ   
vedyānāṃ prathaiva māyākhyaṃ malam | etan māyāmalaṃ sthūlatva   
sūkṣmatva tāratamyena sakalapralayākala vijñānākala   
mantramātṛṣvanusyūtaṃ janmabhogadaṃ kārmaṃ jātyāyurbhogadaṃ   
karmetyuktanītyā pramātuḥ punaḥ punarjananaṃ bhogañca dadāti |   
puṇyā puṇyakartari pramātaribodharahite sati kārmamalam | etat trayaṃ   
māyāśaktyaiva bhavati | asya malatrayasya māyāśaktireva nimittaṃ   
kārmamalaṃ sakalapramātṛṣu teṣāṃ kārmamalepya --------------- kṣā ----  
---- ṇanītyā pralayāt punarutthānarūpaḥ saṃskārarūpeṇāsti   
kārmamalaṃ paramaśivaṃ pratimantramaheśvaramaṃtreśvara   
mantravijñānākala pralayākala sakalākhye pramātṛsaptake   
āṇavamalatāratamye na krameṇa sūkṣmasthūlātmanā tāratamye nāsti |  
  
	cittatvasya pūrṇā hantātmanaḥ prabodharūpaṃ jñātṛkartṛtā   
rūpaṃ sarvajño'haṃ sarvakartāhamityevaṃ bhūtasya svarūpasya   
sthitatve'pi ti ----------- māyayā parityāga āṇavaṃ malaṃ yena male   
nāsau pramātā saṃkucito jātaḥ parimito jātaḥ | atrāṇoḥ   
pūrṇāhantātmanaḥ svarūpasya nimīlanaṃ saṃkocaṃ tat svarūpa   
nimīlanaṃ cidātmani kevalaṃ bodharūpe sthite sati kartṛtva rūpasya   
svātantryātmanaḥ svarūpasyāntarasya nimīlanaṃ kartṛ lakṣaṇe svarūpe   
sthite sati pūrṇāhantātmakaṃ bodhalakṣaṇasya svarūpāntarasya   
nimīlanaṃ vetyubhayaprakāraṃ svarūpāparihāraṃ rūpam āṇavaṃ   
malaṃ dviprakāramadhye ekamevātraiveti āṇave male sati bodhahānitaḥ   
svātantrya hānitaśca dviprakāre svarūpasaṃkoce sati svātmano bhinnasya   
vedyasya prathanaṃ yadbhinnavedya prathā vaśāddharmādharmarūpaṃ   
kārmamalaṃ yataḥ kārmamalājjanma ca bhogaśca bhavati | sa ca bhoga etā   
vantaṃ kālamevamiti niyatā vadhika iti jātyāyurbhogadaṃ (ṭp. 368)   
karmetyuktaṃ bhavati | eṣāmāṇavādi malānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak   
svāśrayasyātmabhūtaḥ pramātṛrūpaṃ sphuṭīkartuṃ   
svātantryāhānirbodhasyetyāṇavamalā prathamabhāmasya prathamaṃ   
sthānāvaśeṣamāha - śuddhacidātmakatve'pi yeṣāṃ   
vijñānakevalānāṃ pramātṝṇāmuttamakartṛtā nāsti te parameśvareṇa   
svātmanaḥ parameśvarādanyonyaṃ ca bhinnā nirmitāḥ   
svātmano'nyonyaṃ ca binnatvena nirmāṇaheturuttamakartṛ tyāgaḥ |   
tasmāt |  
  
	tasmād yeṣāṃ pramātṝṇāṃ bodhaikamātrameva paramārthaḥ   
viśvasyāhamiti svātma viśrāntirūpānandalakṣaṇaṃ svātantryaṃ nāsti |   
prapañce satyapinedamiti parameśvarasvātantrya kalpitādatadabhimānād   
viśvakartāhamiti paraṃ svātantryaṃ nāsti | te parameśvareṇa sarvajñaṃ   
sarvakartṛrūpā pūrṇāhantātmanaḥ svātmanaḥ sakāśāt vyatiriktī   
kṛtāḥ bhinnī kṛtāḥ | eteṣāmetad vyatiriktanirmāṇa hetuḥ   
śivādikṣityanta (475) viśvakartṛtātmakottama svātantryā bhāvāt   
parameśvarasya bodharūpatvaṃ pūrṇāhaṃtātmakottama svātantrya   
viyuktasya mityasya ślokasyābhiprāya śeṣaḥ | kartṛtātyayāddhetoḥ   
parameśvarāt te bhinnā bhavantu vijñānākālānāṃ kathamanyonyaṃ   
bhedaḥ kevalaṃ bādharūpasya vyāpitva dharmakṛta deśā bhedasya   
nityatva dharmakṛtasya kālā bhedasya cānyonyaṃ samānatvāt |  
  
	evamanyonya bhedābhāve nirmitāsta iti kathaṃ   
bahuvacanamityāśaṅkāṃ vyapohati - bodhanityatvasya   
vyāpitvānāmekatve'pi lakṣaṇaṃ tvanyonya bhinnau   
tadvijñānākālavargātmanā parameśvarecchā   
viśeṣeṇānyonyabhinnatā te ca śāstre parameśvareṇa vijñānakevalā   
uktā kartṛtāśūnyaṃ kevalaṃ vijñānamevarūpaṃ yeṣāṃ te,   
tattvavarge śivādikṣityantatattvātmanā śivādi sakalāntapramātrātmanā   
ca bhavitumicchustattadrūpeṇa bhavati prakāśate | natvanyaḥ kaścit   
parameśvara vyatiriktaḥ pramātṛvargo vā kaścinnāstīti | iha yadyat   
kiñcana sphurati tat tad vakṣyamāṇeśvarasvātmaprathā mātra mityādi   
vākyavyākhyānārambhe ātmānamata evāya mityādau cāsakṛduktam |  
  
	yā cidullasati viśvasattayā sā śivo'hamiti viśvasattayā |  
	ākalasya sakṛdevamucyate deśikairasakṛdevamucyate ||  
  
	(ṭp. 369) tataśca sakṛduktatvāt ahaṃ deśakālāsaṃkucitatvād   
vyāpakanityabodhasvabhāvo'pi bhede nānyonya bhinnavijñānā   
kalānātmanā nirbhāse bhātumīśe ityevaṃ bhūteśvarecchā viśeṣeṇa   
teṣāṃ śarīrādi śūnyānta jaḍapramātṛ padottīrṇānāṃ bodhatvādi   
(476) dharmajātasyaikye'pi teṣāmanyonyaṃ bhedaḥ | te ca śāstre   
vijñānakevalā uktāḥ |  tatra vijñānakevalaḥ malaikayukta ityādi granthe   
uktaḥ | vijñānakevalaśabdasyārthaḥ pūrvamevoktaḥ |   
svātantryahānibodhasye tyāṇavamalādi bhāgasya |  
  
	vijñānā kalatā muktvā svātantryasyāpyabodhatā |  
  
	ityamumaṃśaṃ viṣayapradarśanena spaṣṭayati - vijñāne nā   
kalāḥ kalātatvopalakṣita karaṇakāryarahitāḥ sakalapramātṛvat | tasmān   
mahāsauṣuptarūpāt | pralata utthāne karaṇakāryasahitā bhavanti |   
māyātatvāntarvartitvāt teṣāṃ punarutthāna   
lakṣaṇakāraṇakāryabījabhūtaḥ saṃskārātmakārmamalo'pyasti   
madhiyo malaṃ vikalpitaḥ saṃskārātmaka bhinnavedyaviṣaye keṣāṃ cit   
prāṇasuṣupte bhedaprathāmayomayīyomalo'sti | apavedyaviṣaye   
śūnyasuṣupte nāstīti māyīya malovyavasthita viṣayaḥ | yadvakṣyati -   
savedyamapavedyañca māyāmalayutāyutam || iti |  
  
teṣāmāṇava vastu uktakrameṇa svata evāsti | etadapi śabdena sūcitam |  
  
	jaḍatvādabodharūpe śūnye eva yadi vā abodharūpe   
prāṇabodharūpe buddhau vā yeṣāṃ śūnyādāvahamiti camatkāra   
yogāt kartṛtvaṃ te pralaye nā kalāḥ kṛtāḥ kalātatvopalakṣita   
karaṇakāryarahitā ityarthaḥ | pūrṇā hantātmakabodharahitā |   
tasmiñchūnyādau ahaṃ śūnya iti kartāraśca mahāsuṣuptyā vyavahite   
tathāvasthitāḥ pralayādanantaraṃ kāryakāraṇasaṃbaṃdhā eva bhavanti   
yatastataḥ pralayāvadhihite tathā bhūtāsteṣāṃ kevalamuktarūpa āṇava   
evamalaḥ (477) vāsanā saṃskārarūpaḥ bhaviṣyatkāryakāraṇa   
vāsanāsaṃskārarūpatvāt kāryakāraṇodaya hetu dharmā dharmātmā   
ahaṃ puṇyabhāk ahamapuṇyabhāgiti dharmā dharmātmā   
kārmamalo'pyasti | yadyevamiti | kārmamalo'pyasti yadi tat karmahetu   
bhūtā māyāmalātmikā bhinnavedyaprathāpyeṣāṃ syāt |   
satyamityanena bhāgenānu vadati saṃvedye prānisuṣuptapade   
saṃskārātmakavedyasahite prāṇasuṣupte'sti (ṭp. 370) apavedye   
gāḍhasuṣupte na bhavati | bhinna vedya prathāntena sa vedyāpavedya   
sauṣuptapadayorbhinnavedyaprathāyāḥ satvā satvāt vyavasthita viṣayatvena   
māyīyomala eṣāṃ vikalpitaḥ | tathā hītyanena māyā malasya sadbhāvā   
sadbhāvau prakaṭīkaroti | śūnyasyādi apavedyabhāge viśrāntā   
gāḍhanidrayā jaḍī kṛtāḥ apavedye suṣuptipadabhājaḥ kecit pralayā   
kalāḥ | anye tu pralayā kalāḥ buddhiprāṇayoḥ sthitāḥ   
sukhaduḥkhaśeṣarahita sāmānyātmakā bhinnasaṃvedya yoginaḥ   
saṃvedya sauṣuptapadalīnāḥ sthūlasya dehātmanaḥ   
kāryasyendriyātmanaḥ karaṇasya yogarūpatvaṃ sarveṣāṃ tulyam |  
  
	svātantryahānirbodhasyetyāṇavamalasya prathamāṃśo   
vijñānākalaniṣṭhaḥ svātantryāpyabodhatetyayaṃ caramāṃśaḥ   
pralayākalaniṣṭhaḥ | āṇavamalaprasaṃgāt pralayākalasyāpi   
kārmamalaviṣayatvaṃ darśitam | māyāmalasya ca pralayākaleṣu   
pākṣikatvamuktam | evaṃ vijñānākalasyāṇava māyāmalaustaḥ |   
pralayākalasyoktakrameṇamalatrayamastīti bhedamuktvedānīṃ punarāṇava   
kārmamaladvayā bhāve'pi (478) vidyeśvareṣu mantrapramātṛṣu   
māyākhyasya malasya śuddho viṣayo'stīti darśayati -bodhānāṃ   
sarvajñānāmapi bodhakartṛtvajuṣāmahaṃ puṇyakarmā ahaṃ   
pāpakarmeti kārmamalakṣitau sati bhinnavedya yujāṃ teṣāṃ   
māyāmalamastite vidyeśvarāḥ |  
  
	ye pramātāraścinmātramevātmatvena paśyantaḥ māyāpramātṛ   
vajjaḍarūpaṃ dehādyātmatayā paśyanti tasminneva cinmātre ahamiti   
camatkārollāsātkartāraḥ ata eva sarvajñāḥ sarvakartāraḥ   
cinmātrasyaivātmatayā darśanāt | tatraiva kartṛtvāt sarvajñāḥ   
sarvakartāraśca te vidyeśvarāḥ | evaṃ bhūtatve'pi teṣāṃ viśeṣaṃ   
darśayati - kiṃ tvityanena bhuvanabhāvādikaṃ viśvaṃ vedanaviṣayatvāt   
jñānaviṣayatvaṃ vedyatayā kriyā viṣayatvāt kāryatayā ca bhāti |   
māyābhūmau sraṣṭṛrūpāṇāṃ kuvindakumbhakārādīnāṃ tat   
sṛṣṭaṃ vedyaṃ kāryaṃ ca viśvaṃ ghaṭapaṭādi yathā svasmāt   
svātmano bhinnaṃ bhāti | taccedvidyeśvarāṇāṃ vibhinnameva sadbhātīti   
tadbhinnavedyaprathārūpamāyākhya malayogo'sti |  
  
	malatrayasyāpi yau gapadyena sahaiva yo viṣayastaṃ darśayitumāha   
-  
  
	(ṭp. 371) bhavināṃ saṃsāriṇāṃ devādīnāṃ sthāvarāntānāṃ   
vidyādhara devayakṣarākṣasagaṃdharvakinnarāpiśācaguhyakāṇḍaja-   
svedaja jarāyujaudbhijjasarīsṛpasyā varāntānāṃ caturdaśadhā śāstre   
parigaṇitānāṃ trividhaṃ malamasti | teṣu satsvapi kārmamalaṃ teṣāṃ   
devādīnāṃ mukhyatayā saṃsaraṇe saṃsāre kāraṇam | āṇava   
māyāmalau tu kārmeṇa (479) vinā saṃsaraṇe kāraṇaṃ na bhavataḥ | iha   
pramātṛvarge vidyeśvaravijñānākalavargayormāyāntā   
dhvatikrameṇānnannabhavo'sti |   
mantreśvaramantamaheśvaravargayostadadhiṣṭhātrorīśvarabhaṭṭāraka   
sadāśiva bhaṭṭārakayordūrato nāsti pralayākalāstu viśvasaṃhārāt   
punastad viśvodayāntamavidyamānabhāvā māyātatvāntarvartino ye   
devāḥ sthāvarāntāsteṣāṃ trayo'pimalo yugapadeva santi te sarve   
saṃsāriṇa ityuktam | tatra malatrayamadhye katamomalassaṃsaraṇameṣāṃ   
sampādayatītyāśaṃkya kārmamalasyaiva saṃsaraṇasaṃpādanamāha -   
tatrāpi teṣvāpi satsvityarthaḥ | teṣu sat svapi kārmamalaṃ   
pradhānatvenāgatya saṃsaraṇe kāraṇam | yathoktam -   
kārmamalataśśarīrāṇi viṣayāḥ saṃbhavanti | teṣāṃ tanuḥ   
karaṇaviṣayasaṃbaṃdha eva tadānīm | idānīñca vartamānaḥ   
paścātpaścādbhaviṣyaṃścetyanavarata prabandhena vartamānaḥ   
saṃsaraṇamucyate | āṇava māyāmalau tu saṃsāre kāraṇameva |   
āṇavamāyīyau kārmeṇa vināvijñānakevaleṣu kārmamalarahitatvād   
dehādi vicitrabhāvā bhinirvartanaśaktiśūnyau iti mukhyaṃ kārmameva   
malaṃ mukhyaṃ saṃsārakāraṇamiti tatra tatra śāstre bhaṇyate | ata evaṃ   
bhaṇyamānatvāt karmanāśe vṛtte saṃsārasopānapadabaṃdyā   
bhāvodatta ityāśayena sāṃkhyapurāṇabhāratādi śāstreṣu   
karmabandhābhimānaparihāṇireva bhaṇyate |   
ekaikarūpaistribhirdehaistrirūpairdvibhedaiḥ ekarūpatribhedeneti śivādi   
sakalāntāḥ saptapramātāra uttiṣṭhanti | krameṇa tāratamya padavīṃ   
prāptaistribhirāṇavarūpaiḥ kairbhedaiḥ śivamantramaheśvara   
mantreśvarā uttiṣṭhanti | āṇavamāyīyarūpeṇa   
bhedadvayenāṇavakārmarūpeṇaikena bhedena   
mantreśvaravijñānākalapralayākalā (480) yathā kramamuttiṣṭhanti |   
tatrāṇavamāyīya bhedadvayena mantreśvaravijñānā kalā uttiṣṭhanti |   
(ṭp. 372) āṇava kārmātmanā dvibhedena pralayā kalā uttiṣṭhanti | āṇava   
māyīya kārmātmanā ekena bhedena sakalā uttiṣṭhanti | iti malatrayasya   
tribhirekaikabhedaistribhirdvibhedenaikena tribhedena śivādisakalāntāḥ   
saptapramātāraḥ krameṇottiṣṭhanti | tatra malatraye   
sthūlasūkṣmatāratasmya bhedena pradhānatā pradhānatā bhedena   
vikalpabhedena samuccaya bhede nādiśabdena nyūnādhikya bhedena   
cānantaprakāratvamastyeṣāṃ malānām |  
  
	tatra śivamantramaheśvaramantreśvareṣu āṇavaṃ malaṃ   
tāratamyena mukhyam | tatra vidyeśvareṣu yā malasya mukhyatvaṃ   
vijñānākaleṣvāṇa va māyīyayoḥ krameṇamukhyatvaṃ pralayākale   
ṣvāṇava kārmamalayormukhyatvaṃ sakaleṣu malatrayasyaiva mukhyatvam |   
tatrāpi saṃsārahetoḥ kārmamalasyaiva mukhyatvam | etan malamukhyam |   
etadamukhyaṃ taccetacca mukhyamityavāntarabhedo draṣṭavyaḥ | atra ca   
malatrayasya vikāsatirobhedāt saṃsāriṇāṃ baṃdhamokṣātmakaṃ   
prakāradvayaṃ darśayati |  
  
	kalāśaktyātmanā tattve nopadbalitaṃ malenanyakkṛtaṃ   
sarvarūparahito'haṃ tṛṣito'haṃ pipāsito'haṃ sukhyahaṃ duḥkhyahaṃ   
kṛśo'haṃ shtūlo'hamityatra cidrūpaṃ śūnyadehāntaraṃ   
pradhānīkṛtyasvaṃ pradhānatvena sthitam | tatra hetu māha - mitaṃ   
idantāpannaṃ kiñca dehādiśūnyānta pramātṛbhāganimagnatvācca   
prameyaṃ yadā punaḥ kartṛtāyāścidātmano bodhasya mukhyatvaṃ   
śūnyādāvetajjñātṛ kartṛtvayorapradhānatvena sthite sati tajjñānaṃ   
parameśvarātmaka svasvarūpasamāveśalakṣaṇam |  
  
	(481) etacceti | bhavināṃ tridaśādīnāṃ caitanyaṃ yad   
dehādāvātmano bodhabhāgasya nimajjitatvāt kartṛtāmayaṃ cidrūpasya   
tatvamiti svātantryamityarthaḥ | parameśvaraśaktyātmanā kalākhyena   
kiñcitkartṛtārūpeṇa tattvena upodvalitamanuprāṇitaṃ malena nyak kṛtaṃ   
sadudbodhitaṃ śūnyādi dehānta māyā pramātṛ saṃbandhi yat tatvaṃ   
svātantryaṃ śūnyādipradhānīkṛtya svayamapradhānatvena sthitaṃ   
tadidantāṃ prāptam | kiñca dehādiśūnyānta   
prameyabhāganimagnatvācca prameyaṃ yogaura iti dehasya sukhīti buddheḥ   
yastṛṣita iti prāṇasya yaḥ (ṭp. 373) sarvarūparahita iti śūnyasya gauroyaḥ   
sohamiti gaurādirūpā idantai vāṃ tarhitāhaṃ bhāvā bhūtvā   
saṃsāriṇyaṃ parisphurati seyaṃ saṃsārāvasthā   
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptarūpā yaḥ khalvahamiti bhāti sa ---- pūrṇaḥ svatantro   
vibhurnityaḥ sapūrṇasvatantra ityuktagurupadeśayuktibhiḥ | nityo'haṃ   
paripūrṇohaṃ svatantro'hamahaṃ vibhuḥ |  
  
	ityevaṃ vimṛśannāse satyena vacasā guruḥ ||  
  
	iti nītyā svātantryātmakatva nityatvādi dharmaparāmarśātmani   
cidrūpe vidadhatā te naiva paripūrṇe nāhaṃ bhāvena śūnyādiṃ   
prameyaṃ saṃvit svarūpe nimajjyaivāsya te yadā tadā turyātītāvasthā |   
yadā tu parāmṛṣṭastadā(thā) bhūtavaibhavanityatvaiśvaryādi saṃbhede   
naivāhaṃ bhāvena śūnyādi dehāntaṃ saptadhātūṃśca siddhasya   
mantrasiddhena raso yathā tāmrādi svarṇī bhavati tadvacchūnyādi   
dehadhātvantaṃ siddharasena na (482) vidhyate | sā turyadaśā tadā tasyāṃ   
turyadaśāyāṃ tadapi śūnyādi prameyatāmujjhatīva saṃvinmayī   
bhāvāt turyāvasthā turyātītāvasthā ceti dvayapi jīvanmuktyavasthā   
samāveśa ityuktā | śāstre saṃvicchāstre tatra tatrāgame'hantā   
rūpasamyagāveśanameva hi pradhānāveśasiddhaye upadeśāntarāṇi   
samāveśopāya viśeṣākārāṇyapekṣaṇīyāni | yathā gītaṃ bhagavatā -   
māyipūrṇāhantātmani svarūpe manaḥ dehāderapyupalakṣaṇam |   
māyimana āveśya nimajjya - mayyāveśyamano ye māṃ nityayuktā   
upāsate | śraddhayā parayopetāste me yuktatamā matāḥ ||  
iti nityayuktā avirataṃ svasvarūpasamāveśodyuktāḥ te mahāyogino   
matāḥ ||  
  
	athāveśāyituñcittaṃ na śaknomi mayi sthiram |  
	abhyāsayogena tato mabhicchāptuṃ dhanañjayaḥ ||  
  
	iti ca dehaprāṇabuddhiśūnyādi prahvībhāvo'nuprāṇitāḥ   
parameśvarastuti prāṇāḥ pūjā dhyānasamādhiprabhṛtayaḥ   
sameveśapallavā aṃśā iti prasiddhāḥ | samāveśābhyāse'samarthaḥ   
san matkarmaparamo bhāvaḥ,  
  
	madarthamayi karmāṇi kurvan siddhimavāpsyasi | iti dehapāte (ṭp.   
374) parameśvaraikarasa iti kaḥ kutra kathaṃ samāviśet |   
svavyatirekeṇānyasyā bhāvāt svayameva parameśvaratvāt | tadetaduktaṃ   
prameyamatyāha | kartṛtāyāḥ pūrṇāhantātmikāyāḥ kartṛtāyā   
mukhyatvaṃ yat kartṛtāyā avinābhāvaḥ śūnyo darguṇabhāvaḥ   
acidrūpe śūnyādau guṇī bhūte svātantryasyāpyabodhatetyuktasya mala   
vyāpārasyā bodhatetyuktasyāṇava malavyāpārasyāpahastanāt   
bodhātmakaścito (483) parodhabhogo yaḥ āṇavamalenanyak kṛto'bhūt   
tasyāpi bodhalakṣaṇasya bhāgasyādhunāpi   
kartṛtonmajjanakāle''cchādakasyāṇava malanyagbhāvād   
bodhasyonmagnatvena mukhyatvaṃ bhavati | kartṛtāyā mukhyatvaṃ   
yadunmagnatvaṃ kartṛtva bodhayorunmagnameva jñānam | asya   
samāveśalakṣaṇasya jñānasyā jñānātmaka malapratipakṣatvāt tadetat   
kartṛtva bodhayo svasvarūpasamāveśātmakaṃ mukhyatvam | yena   
samāveśena dehe sthito'pi pramātāpatiriti tamukta iti śāstreṣūktaḥ |   
patidaśāyāṃ pramātusturyatadatītarūpā ca daśā evamukta prakāreṇa   
bhavatu | pramātuḥ paśudaśāyāṃ suṣupta svapnajāgrad daśā āgameṣu   
kathamuktamityāśaṃkyaślokatreṇasuṣupta svarūpameva   
prathamamācaṣṭe |  
  
	buddhiprāṇadehaghaṭādyabhāvātmani śūnyo'hamityahantā   
kartṛtā yāḥ pade āspade asphuṭa ārūpe asphuṭe   
cidrūpabuddhiprāṇadehasaṃskāramātriṇe śūnye jñeyānāṃ   
śūnyatā bhavati | sā jñeyaśūnyatā akṣāṇāṃ cakṣurādīndriyāṇāṃ   
saṃskāramātrarūpā antarmukhīvṛttiḥ prāṇādiprerikā   
prāṇāpānasamānodāna vyānātmani vāyucakraprerikā sā jñeya   
śūnyā jīvanākhyā matā jīvatīti jīvanākhyā sā śaktiḥ |   
  
	athavā prāṇasauṣupte puryaṣṭakātmikā ahantā jīvanākhyā   
bhavati | tāvanmātra sthitau śūnyatāmātra sthitau proktaṃ pralayopamaṃ   
prāṇasauṣuptaṃ māyāmalayuktatvāt (484) saṃskāravedyasahitaṃ   
māyāmalayuktatvād eva vedyaṃ sauṣuptaṃ tāvan mātra sthitau   
śūnyamātra sthitau proktam |  
  
	iha cittattvaṃ svasvarūpamācchādayan jñeyarūpeṇa buddhyādinā   
jñeyarūpo dehāntena (ṭp. 375) ghaṭādinā cā bhāsate |   
cittatvasyaivamadvitīyaṃ svātantryavijṛmbhitam | atra svātantrya vijṛṃbhite   
vāstavaṃ vasturūpaḥ kramo vā bhedo vā nāsti | tatrāpi   
kramabhedayorabhāve'pi cittatvasya svātantryāt kramaśca   
bhedaścābhāsate | paramārthato deśakālakramābhāvādabhede'pi   
bhedaśca kramaścābhāsate | iti sthite yaccittatvasya   
svarūpācchādanabhāgaḥ sa śūnyabhāgaḥ uttarottara   
buddhiprāṇadeharūpeṇa bhāgāntareṇā saṃkīrṇā yadā viśrāmyati   
tatraiva śūnyabhāge ahantārūpakartṛtāyāḥ padaṃ parāmarśaḥ   
buddhiprāṇādīnāsphuṭatvādī ṣadrūpātmanā vedyapadavīmāptena ata   
eva śuddhasaṃskāreṇa parāmarśaḥ ahantāyāḥ katṛtārūpaḥ   
parāmarśo yokto bhavati yadā tadā saiva śūnyā va   
sthānetyabhāvāmarśaśeṣā | anīpsitaṃ niṣedhya buddhyādiṣu   
suspaṣṭasaṃbhedāpi buddhirnāsti deho nāsti ghaṭādirnāsti iti   
niṣedharūpaḥ suspaṣṭaparāmarśasaṃbhedaḥ apekṣito'pi niyataḥ bhāvi   
niṣedhya yogāt akiñcano'hamityevaṃ bhūtaparāmarśavat mama   
kiñcidapi nāstīti svīkṛtasāmānyākāra niṣedhyā ata eva   
sāmānyākāraniṣedhyarūpatvāt saṃskāraśeṣīkṛta jñeyarūpā   
śūnyāvasthetyucyate | tathā vidyasaṃskāraśeṣīkṛta   
buddhyāderdehāntasya saṃskāraśeṣīkṛtasya nīlāderabhāvarūpe   
śūnya ityucyate | yasmāt tatra śūnye jñeyānāṃ śūnyatā   
abhāvarūpatā saṃskāra śeṣatā saṃskāra viśeṣa taiva sarvatrābhāvaḥ   
satāṃ vastūnāṃ sarvātmanā na vināsaḥ tatra śūnyapramātari   
saṃyuktā avinābhūtā prāṇādyātmake vāyucakre   
preraṇātmikāśaktistatraiva samacetā sā śaktiḥ   
vidyākalātatvayorvikāsabhūmau krameṇa vidyāyāḥ prapañcabhūtaḥ   
buddhindriyavargaḥ kalāyāḥ prapañcabhūtaḥ karmendriyavarga iti   
krameṇabuddhīndriyavargeṇa vargau yau tayo buddhindriya   
karmendriyayostayorāntarīvṛttiḥ   
tayorbuddhīndriyayostayorāntarīvṛttistayorbuddhīndriyavargayoḥ   
śabdasparśādeḥ parāmarśarūpāḥ śabdasparśarūparasagandhānām   
abhivyaktirūpasya sthānasyābhihananādi rūpā bāhyā vṛttiḥ   
sāmānyakaraṇavṛttiḥ prāṇādyā vāyavaḥ pañcaprāṇādyāḥ   
pañcavāyavaḥ karaṇānāṃ sāmānyā yā sādhāraṇīvṛttiḥ (ṭp. 376)   
śūnye indriyacakropodbalikā jīvanamiti śūnya eva jīvaḥ saṃsaratīti yaḥ   
rūpādi vā | athavendriya śaktīnāmāntarī sādhāraṇaprāṇanātmikā   
prāṇaśabdavācyā prāṇādimārutaviśeṣapreraṇāmayī vṛttiryā tadā   
saivaśaktirahamityatiśayyamānā prāṇapramāturjīvanaṃ yadā tadā   
prāṇa eva jīvaḥ saṃsārītyarthaḥ | śūnyapramātā prāṇapramātā ca   
pūryaṣṭakaśabdavācyaḥ prāṇādipañcakaṃ pratyekamekaṃ   
buddhīndriyavarga ekaḥ niścayātmikā ca dhīryataḥ śūnyarūpāt   
prāṇarūpācca pramāturvyajyata iti svamate pūryaṣṭakam |   
  
	matāntaramapyāha - tanmātrapañcakaṃ ca   
mano'haṅkārabuddhayaḥ ityanye | tanmātrodayarūpeṇa mano'haṃ   
buddhivartinā puryaṣṭakena saṃruddha iti |  
  
	bhūmirāpo'nalo vāyuḥ svaṃ mano buddhireva ca |  
	(485) ahaṅkāra itī yaṃ me bhinnā prakṛtiraṣṭadhā || ityanye |  
  
śūnyātmakaṃ prāṇātmakaṃ pūryaṣṭakaṃ yat tāvativedya sparśā   
bhāvāt śuddhe ubhayātmake śūnyapramātuḥ prāṇapramātuḥ   
viśrāntistasyāṃ viśrāntau satyāṃ viśeṣeṇa suṣuptā yā ahantā yā   
bodhātmakaṃ bhāvarūpaṃ suṣuptā yāḥ bhāvaḥ sauṣuptamiti suṣuptā   
yā ahantā yā (bodhātmakaṃ bhāvarūpaṃ) karma ca sauṣuptaṃ   
tadbhāvakarmakarmātmakaṃ sauṣuptaṃ jāgratsvapnayorapi malena   
pramātā suptaḥ kiñcitkartṛrūpayā kalayā asupta iva sauṣupte tannimajjane   
suṣuptasya bhāvaḥ karma ca sauṣuptamiti | tatra ca śūnyasauṣupte   
prāṇasparśakṛtasya sukhaduḥkhāderastitvāt māyākhyaṃ malamasti |   
atastatsauṣuptaṃ savedyamapavedya savedyasuṣuptavat pralayo'pimantavyaḥ |   
pralayaḥ dehādipradhvaṃsānudayābhyāṃ kṛtaścirakālaśca   
dehādervidyamānatve'pi dehādyanādaraṇe kṛtaṃ sauṣuptamacirakālaṃ   
ceti śeṣaḥ | tatra sauṣuptaśramakṛtaṃ suṣuptaṃ nidrādhātudoṣa kṛtaṃ   
sauṣuptamūrcchādravya kṛtaṃ sauṣuptaṃ madonmadādi svātantrya   
kṛtaṃ sauṣuptaṃ samādhiryogaḥ ityavāntarabhedāḥ ||  
  
	kecittu - samādhirūpaṃ sauṣuptaṃ savedyam | anyāni   
sauṣuptānyapavedyānīti kecidāhuḥ | idaṃ sukhaṃ idaṃ duḥkhaṃ ayaṃ   
dehaḥ ayaṃ prāṇa iyaṃ buddhiriti sphuṭādvedyasthānādvinirmuktāyāḥ   
(ṭp. 377) suṣuptāvasthāyāḥ śūnye buddhyādyabhāvādyā ityādi   
ślokatrayoktanītyā (487) suṣuptāvasthāyāḥ svarūpamastu | idānīṃ   
nīlamityādi sphuṭavedyābhāsayoginyoḥ svapnajāgraddaśayoranyonyaṃ   
ko bheda ityāśaṅkyaślokadvayena bhedamāha - antaḥkaraṇātmani mano   
mātre mārge'pi svapne ahaṃ cakṣuṣā kāntārūpaṃ dṛṣṭvān   
śravaṇena śabdaṃ śrutavān ityādi rūpeṇa bhrāntyā sphuṭa prakāśā   
bhāvānāṃ āntarī asthirā asādhāraṇī pārameśvarī sṛṣṭiḥ paśoḥ   
pramātuḥ svapnāvasthāmatā | āgameṣu parameśvareṇoktā   
paramārthataścakṣurādi sarvākṣaviṣayatvena yā sṛṣṭiḥ pramātuḥ   
bāhyarūpā sthirā sarvapramātṝṇāṃ sādhāraṇī sā   
sṛṣṭirjāgarāvasthā | cakṣurādindriyādhiṣṭhānāni   
dṛḍhaniyatāvāsabhūtāni cakṣurgolakāśravaṇaśaṣkulī ityādīni   
nidrāyamāṇasya nimīlitāni lakṣyante | adhiṣṭhāna nabhūta   
cakṣurgolakādiṣu nimīliteṣu satsubāhyendriyavyāpāro na dṛṣṭaḥ   
kaścidapi śeṣaḥ | tena dṛṣṭatvā bhāvāt cakṣurādīndriya   
vyāpārānapekṣe kevalaṃ manormāgre cakṣurādīndriya viṣaya   
sparśādayo bhāvāḥ akṣādīndriyagrahaṇasamucite na spaṣṭena vapuṣā   
bhāsamānayogyāḥ santaḥ svapne parameśvareṇa sṛjyate | natvaṇunā   
svapnāvasthā vatā na | aṇunā sṛjyate cet anirdiṣṭasyavastuno darśanaṃ na   
bhavati | tasmādaṇunā na sṛjyate | iṣṭasya vastuno darśane'pi   
svātmanādhiṣṭhita deśaṃ tatra vartamānaṃ kālaṃ tatra   
vartamānamākāraṃ vihāyānyadeśakālādiyogena darśanāt svayaṃ tat   
svapnāvasthā vatā na sṛjyata iti śeṣaḥ | ata eva pārameśvarāduktarūpāt   
sargādeva manomātrasthitatvādeveyaṃ rūpasparśādīnāṃ sṛṣṭiḥ   
pramātrantaradhāriṇī na bhavati | svapnadraṣṭureva saṃbandhinī   
tādṛśyāṃ (488) satyāmasādhāraṇyāṃ sṛṣṭau rūpasparśādīnāṃ   
cakṣurādīndriya viṣayatvaṃ svavyatiriktacaitramaitrādi pramātrantara   
sādhāraṇyaṃ cakāsti | tad dvayamapi yāvad bhavati tāvat tathaiva   
bhānaparyantaṃ tathaiva bhāsanaparyantaṃ yadyapi paramārthameva tathā   
māpamānatvāt tathāpi paramārthamapi uttarakālaṃ prabuddhasya   
cakṣurādīndriyaviṣayatvaṃ svavyatirikta caitramaitrādi pramātrantara   
sādhāraṇyaṃ (ṭp. 378) cakāstītyuttarakālaparāmarśena tad dvayarūpaṃ   
nirmūlya mānatvenāvabhātīti bhrāntaṃ svapataḥ pramātustasmin svapne   
svātmanā saha caitramaitrapramātrantarāṇi cakṣurādi bāhyendriyāṇi ca   
bhānti | tāni prabodhakālabhāvibhiḥ pramātrantaraiścakṣurādibhiś-  
cābhinnānīti | tatra svapne niścayaḥ prabodhakāle tathā na | etaiḥ   
pramātrantarai cakṣurādibhiścābhinnāni na iti tadabheda   
niścayānuvṛttirapohyata eva pramātrantarasādhāraṇaniścayamānaṃ   
cakṣurādīndriya mānamityubhayaṃ bhrāntameva | śuktyāṃ   
rajatabuddhivat ubhayorvastunorbhāntamevāsthairyarūpasparśādīnāṃ   
sṛṣṭe sūtroktena cakṣurāditrayaviṣayatvā bhāve naivā   
sādhāraṇatvamākṣiptaṃ vibhramāditi sūtroktena padenāsthairyamiti   
svamukhe noktamācāryeṇa tadasthairyasvapnapratiyogi jāgradavasthā   
svarūpanirūpaṇāvasare'pi darśitaṃ darśayiṣyatītyarthaḥ | uktarūpā   
asādhāraṇī sṛṣṭiryā sā pārameśvarī sṛṣṭiḥ svapnasamaye bhāvāt   
svapnataḥ kāle'pi viṣayatvaṃ pramātrantara sādhāraṇyaṃ ca   
niścayānuvṛttyā | ata eva bādhā virahitayā satyatvena cakāsti | ata eva   
bādhāvirahitayā cakāsanāt bāhyākṣaviṣayā pramātrantara sādhāraṇī   
ca sṛṣṭiḥ paśorjāgaraḥ tat sṛṣṭiviṣayaṃ pramātṛtvaṃ paśoḥ   
jāgarāvasthā (489) ghaṭapaṭādi viṣaya niścaya jñānasyānuvṛtteḥ   
sthairyaṃ yāvaccakāsti jāgaro'pitāvat | taccakāsanāvadhijāgaraḥ   
madhye kālāntare'pi smṛtyāniścayānuvṛttinirmūlanāt jāgradapi svapna   
eva | vastūnāmasphuṭā sphuṭarūpā va bhāsasāratvādanubhūtasya   
vastunaḥ kālāntare'pi smṛtyā sphuṭatvā bhāvāt tadanubhavataścārūpo   
jāgradapi kālāntare svapna eva bhavati | yatra dīrghadīrghe'pi yat   
svapnāntaraṃ bhavati dīrgha dīrgha svapnā pekṣayā tadānīṃ bhavat   
svapnamapi jāgradeva svapne jāgradabhimatadīrghadīrghamapi   
svapnāntaraṃ niścayānuvṛtti tirodhānā tatraiva tadānīṃ   
bhavajjāgradabhimata svapnāpekṣayā svapna eveti mantavyam |  
  
	āsāṃ jāgradādyavasthānāṃ heyatvaṃ pradarśayan   
turyaturyātītātmakamavasthā (ṭp. 379) dvayamupādeyamiti sūcayati -   
iyamiti | śūnye buddhyādityādi ślokapaṃcake nokta sauṣuptāvasthā trayī   
heyā | kasmāddhetoriti cet kartṛtā yā guṇībhūtatve prāṇādeḥ   
prādhānyāt tayoḥ prāṇādi kartṛtayorhāno pacaya   
prāyasukhaduḥkhādeḥ saṃ bhavat prāṇādernyagbhāve kartṛtāyā   
upacayaḥ katṛtāyā nyagbhāve prāṇāderūpacaya iti yasminnavasthā traye   
kasyācit tyāgaḥ kasyacidupādānaṃ tayoḥ tyāgo pādānayoricchātyāgo   
pādānārthaprayatnamādiśabdābhimānamityādikaṃ parikleśaṃ paśyati   
| tadavasthā trayamasyāḥ pramāturheyatābhāti saparikleśaḥ   
sukhaduḥkhayoryogavaicitryeṇaiva kṛtastadvaicitryamavasthā traye   
saṃbhavati yataḥ ataḥ avasthā trayaṃ heyam |   
  
	(490) tat saṃbhavahetumāha - kartṛtārūpamātmaviśrāntya   
nanyonmukhalakṣaṇamānandaikaghanaṃ cinmayaṃ vapuḥ | taccinmayaṃ   
vapuryadā prāṇādi traye śūnye pūryaṣṭake dehādi bhūmiṣu ca   
guṇatāmabhyeti | tasmin cidrūpavapuṣi guṇībhūte sati prāṇādeḥ   
prādhānyaṃ sphurati cidrūpasya yathā yathā hāniḥ tathā tathā   
sukhaduḥkhodayaścidrūpasya yathā yathā kiñcidunmajjanaṃ tathā tathā   
sukhodayaḥ |  
  
	tat saṃbhavameva pratipādayati - bubhukṣā kāle   
prāṇasyodrekācidrūpasya nimajjanatvād duḥkhaṃ tṛptau   
prāṇādernyagbhāvādahantodreke sukhaṃ śrāntasya spandanā   
spandanayoścalanā calanayoḥ calane dehasya prādhānyaṃ viśrāntau   
cidrūpasya prādhānyam | yastu cidānandaghana svasvarūpa   
samāveśatatvajño yastasya samāveśa bubhukṣākāle duḥkhānudaya eva |  
  
	durbalo'pi tadākramya yataḥ kāle pravartate |  
	ācchādayed bubhukṣāṃ ca tathā yo'ti bubhukṣitaḥ ||  
  
	tat spandātmakaṃ balamākramya kārye pravartate ||  
  
ityaśakyamapi vastu sādhayati | samāveśa tatvajño yaḥ ati bubhukṣitaḥ   
bubhukṣāmācchādayet prāṇādi prādhānye prayāsabhūmiṃ   
duḥkhayogaṃ kartṛtāyāṃ nyagbhāva iti trayaṃ jāgratsvapna   
suṣuptātmakaṃ trayaṃ heyameva | kartṛtā prādhānye prayāsabhūmiṃ   
(ṭp. 380) duḥkhayogaṃ kartṛtāyāḥ prādhānye prayāsabhūmiṃ   
sukhayogaḥ jāgradādiṣu prāṇādiprādhānyaṃ kartṛtāyāṃ nyagbhāva   
iti trayaṃ jāgratsvapna suṣuptātmakaṃ trayaṃ heyameva kartṛtā   
prādhānyonmeṣāt turyarūpāt prabhṛti tat sthairyātmaka turyātīta   
sthairyātmaka turyātīta daśāntamupādeyam |   
ekarasānandaghanasvabhāvalābhe upādātumicchā jihā sā (491)   
etayorvivaśā bhāva pariśramāt |  
  
	turyaṃ turyātītaṃ copadeyamiti tātparyam | avasthātrayasya   
prāṇādiprādhānyaṃ heyatāyāṃ kāraṇamuktaṃ tat prāṇādi   
prādhānyaṃ jāgradādi traya eva cet tarhi turyādau prāṇādi prādhānyā   
bhāvāt turyatadatītarūpātmani samāveśe prāṇādi   
pramātrātmakasyacyute ranupapattiḥ caitramaitrādi bhūmikāroho na bhavet   
| dehādi kāluṣyarahita parameśvarātmaka svasaṃvidrūpa samāviṣṭatvāt   
punarapi sabhavatyevetyāśaṃkyāha - suptajāgrato paraḥ pūrṇā   
śivādikṣityanta viśvaprāṇanarūpaḥ parāśaktiḥ spandātmakaḥ paraḥ   
prāṇaḥ |  
  
	guṇādi spandaniṣpandāḥ sāmānyaspandasaṃśrayāt |  
	labdhātmalābhaḥ satataṃ syūrjñasyāparipanthinaḥ ||  
  
iti śrīspandoktanītyā pramātuḥ svapnajāgarāvasthayoḥ pratyekaṃ   
prāṇāpānamayaḥ sūryacandramayaśca sakalapramātrātmakaśca   
supte'pi prāṇāpānamayaḥ jāgratyapi prāṇāpānamayaḥ saparaprāṇaḥ   
pramātuḥ sauṣupte suṣuptāvasthāyāṃ kaṃcit kālaṃ tacchedātmā   
prāṇāpānacchedātmā tayornirindriyapradeśe hṛdayasadane kaṃcitkālaṃ   
viśramaṇātmāsamānākhyo bhavati | sauṣupte prāṇāpānātmaka sūryā   
candramasorubhayorapi viśrāntyātmaka samānākhyaḥ pralayakālaḥ   
pramātrātmakaśca | viṣuvatsviva viṣuvatkālatulyaḥ   
unnatādhikyarahitadinarātrisāmānyātmakaṃ   
dakṣiṇottaragativiśramaṇātmakaviṣuvatkālatulyaḥ |  
  
	kiñcidinarātryorūnatādhikyarūpaṃ viśeṣaṃ suvati avirataṃ   
prerayatīti viṣuvadvāmadakṣiṇamārgau | iḍāpiṅgalamārgau khilīkṛtya   
madhyamārgeṇordhvaṃ (492) gacchati yadā sa eva prāṇaḥ |   
tadānīmudānākhya sūryagaḥ turyāgataḥ (ṭp. 381) (492) hutabhuṅmayaḥ   
svāntaḥ sthitaḥ vijñānākalamantreśvaramantramaheśvara   
tadadhiṣṭhātṛrūpānantabhaṭṭārakarūpaśca turyātītakaḥ prāṇaḥ   
viśvātmakaḥ paraḥ paramaśivātmakaḥ prāṇaḥ iti śivādikṣityantaṃ   
viśvaṃ svāveśena jīvayantī cidrūpasya paramaśivasya   
parābhaṭṭārikārūpā sthitiryā sā tāvat sāmānyaparispandarūpā   
śivādi dharaṇyantaviśvasādhāraṇaparispandarūpā stūlo'haṃ   
kṛśo'haṃ balo'haṃ durbalo'haṃ iti svātantryāropaṇasāraṃ sati, ata eva   
sthūla evāhaṃ na kṛśa iti kalparūpaḥ parāmarśamayī saiva citrarūpa   
sthitiṃ prāṇāpānasamānodānavyānātmanā pañcarūpatāṃ bhajate |   
tatra pañcarūpatā bhajane kiṃcijjahatī kvacit patantī cāntararūpaṃ   
tyaktvā bahiḥ patantī bahīrūpaṃ tyaktvā antaḥ patantī krameṇa praśvāsa   
niśvāsarūpā prāṇatvātmakamapānatvātmakaṃ ca viśeṣaṃ darśayati |   
ucchvāsarūpaḥ prāṇaḥ āntararūpaṃ tyaktvā bahirviṣaye patati | apānaḥ   
niśvāsarūpaḥ bahīrūpaṃ tyaktvā antaḥ patati | ubhayorapi tyāgapatane   
tulye | tadidaṃ viśeṣadvayaṃ prāṇatvamapānatvañca viśeṣadvayaṃ   
jāgarāvasthāyāṃ jāgrataḥ pramātuḥ svātmanaḥ sphuṭameva |   
sphuṭatvameva darśayati - dehāt prasṛtya viṣaye viśvāntestato viṣayāt   
prasṛtya dehe viśrānteḥ etadanubhavadaśāyāṃ smṛtyanusaṃdhānadaśā   
manasaḥ prasṛtya ābhyantara eva vedye viśrānteḥ | tataśca prasṛtyamanasi   
viśrānteḥ jāgradavasthāyāṃ prāṇāpānayoḥ suṣpaṣṭatvāt svapne'pi   
prāṇāpānatvamastyeva | svapato'pihi pramātuḥ   
nisargamapraveśātmānau prāṇāpānau sphuṭameva (493) pārśva sthitau   
pramātrā lakṣye te | svayamapi svātmanā svapne'ntaḥ sphurad   
vedyasaṃvedanāt tyāgopādānarūpā sthitiḥ saṃpādyate | manasā   
nirgatya tasminneva vedye patanāt tyāgopādānarūpā sthitiḥ saṃpadyate |   
tena viśeṣa dvayasya svīkārāt pramānāśaktiḥ jāgrati   
prāṇāpānaviśeṣadvayamayī yathā tathā svapne   
prāṇāpānaviśeṣadvayamayī suptaṃ svapnaḥ supte pramātari tadeva   
suptaṃ (ṭp. 382) yadā sutarāṃ sphuṭaṃ bhavati tadā suṣuptaḥ pramātā   
suṣuptasya padaṃ sauṣuptapadaṃ prāṇasauṣuptaṃ ----------- nya   
sauṣuptamiti dvividham | samānarūpaṃ paraprāṇīyaṃ viśeṣaṃ svīkaroti   
| savedye prāṇe sauṣupte prāṇāpānayoḥ spando lakṣyate | tathāpi tayoḥ   
prāṇāpanayoryā madhye viśrāntiḥ indriyāt tena hṛdayasadane viśrāntiḥ   
prāṇāpānamayoḥ mukhyataḥ sauṣuptaṃ tatra sauṣupte kañcit kālaṃ   
prāṇāpānayorvicchedaḥ viśrāntiḥ | tadātmā viśrāntyātmā   
ardyamānasya parvādaṃ sādi padārthasya śarīrāntaḥ ūrdhvapradeśe   
tiryakṣu ca samānavyāpārātmā samānīkaraṇa vyāpārātmakatvāt   
hṛtpadmavikāsadānāt bhuktapītajaraṇakārī bhavati | samānaḥ   
dinarātrirūpayoḥ prāṇāpānayoḥ kañcitkālaṃ sāmyāt   
prāṇāpānayorvicchedādviṣuvatkālatulyaḥ viṣuṃ vyāptaṃ   
samānīkaraṇarmahatīti vatistato'rhārthatvād avyayatvaṃ nāsti | taddhi   
udgato nivata iti prasiddhatvaṃ nyāyasiddhaṃ vedanyāyasiddhaṃ na   
prayoktavyam | atra śāstratvāt prayuktameva vā |  
  
	athavā dinarātrautayorūnādhikatvalakṣaṇaṃ viśeṣaṃ   
suvatiprerayatyaviratamiti śatariviṣuvat | tatra viṣuvati vicchidyamānasya   
prāṇāpānasya (494) saṃskārarūpatayā sadbhāvaḥ |   
saṃskārarūpatayā sadbhāva eva vicchedaḥ śūnye buddhyādyabhāvā   
ityādāvuktaṃ hānādānayoḥ prāṇāpānayoḥ suṣupte nījarūpatā asti   
iyati samānamātre sakalaḥ pralayākalātaḥ paśuvargaḥ paśuñca   
prāṇakāraṇabhūtā prāṇanāvṛtti iḍāpiṅgalamārgaukhilībhāvayantī   
madhyamanāḍyordhvarūpayā pravahati yadā tadā   
tadūrdhvamārgapravahaṇaṃ samastabhedasya ahaṃ caitra eva namaitraḥ   
ghaṭa eva na paṭaḥ ityādi samastabhedasthā bhedasāratā   
dānalakṣaṇamāśyānasya sarpiṣo vilāpanamiva vijñānākalādārabhya   
sadāśivāntaṃ pravahaṇaṃ vidadhatī udānavṛttirbhavati | sā   
udānavṛttisturyātmikā daśāmāyordhvaṃ vijñānākala iti   
vijñānākalādārabhyabhedagalanaṃ pravartate | bhede (ṭp. 383) vilīne sati   
ghaṭapaṭādi sarvavedyarāśirūpatatvasakalādi   
pramātṛbhogabhūmibhuvanavargātmaka viśvadeha vyāpanarūpeṇa   
prāṇanāvṛttirudānarūpā viśvātmakaparamaśivocitaturyātītarūpā   
bhavati prāṇapramātaiva jāgratsvapnayoḥ prāṇāpānarūpaḥ   
sauṣuptasamānarūpaḥ turye udānarūpaḥ turyātīte vyānarūpa iti   
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ prāṇapramātai vā sā vudānaḥ   
vijñānākalaścāsau mantraścāsau vijñānākalavargāpekṣayā   
mantrapramātṛtadīśatanmaheśamātrapekṣayā tat   
pramātṛvargādhiṣṭhātrapekṣayā ca vyavahriyate |  
  
	etacclokadvayāvataraṇā vasaraprayukta śaṅkāparihārāya   
ślokadvayatātparyamāha - etaduktamiti | turyatadatītayoḥ   
pañcaprāṇamayī prāṇanāśaktirastyeva | anyathā nāsti cet   
samāveśāvasarānantaraṃ pramāturjīvatvabahirmukhavyāpārarūpasya   
vyutthānasya cānupapattesturyatadatītayostathāpi prāṇānāśaktau (495)   
satyāmapi turīye bhedopasaṃhāratvāt turyātīte abhedaviśrānti   
pradhānatvādanayosturyaturyātītayossukhaduḥkhādivaicitryābhāvād   
ekarūpasvātmaviśramātmakaparamānandamayatvād upādeya taiva |   
suṣuptādau tu sukhaduḥkhādi vaicitryarūpasya bhedasya   
saṃskārarūpatvāt svapnajāgratoḥ sphuṭavedyollāsasya bhedasya ca   
vidyāmānatvādasti sukhaduḥkhādivaicitryamiti tāsu jāgratādiṣu daśāsu   
heyataiveti heyātrayī yāmityuktaṃ yuktameva | viśvaśarīrasya bhagavataḥ   
paramaśivasya prāṇādipañcarūpataiva sakalātmaka   
pramātṛgatāntarbahirantarudyogapraveśarūpatā jāgratsvapnāvasthayoḥ   
sakalaprāṇāpānarūpā sauṣupte pralayākalavargocita samānarūpāturye   
vijñānakalādi sadāśivāntapramātṛvargocito dānarūpā turyātīte   
śivadaśocita vyānarūpā ityanena sūtradvayena |   
yathoktamāgameṣaṭtriṃśadityādi |  
  
iti dvitīyamāhnikam ||  
  
  
  
(ṭp. [384] 394) atha --------------------------------------  
  
anantabhāgameyādi vaicitryasvīkāre'pi ātmānaṃ   
bhedaśālinamātmatvena prathayate - viśvottīrṇaṃ   
pūrṇāhantātmakamātmānaṃ yaḥ prathayate bhaktānāṃ   
pratyabhijñāta svātmamaheśvarasamāviṣṭānāṃ   
śivādikṣityantānantatatvamayamānamiti mātṛcakraṃ ca   
bhaktānāmapyātmānaṃ yo'tyaikyena prathayate avirataṃ (496) prakaṭī   
karoti yastaṃ śivaṃ stumaḥ |  
  
	evamiti | uktaprakāreṇa jñānādhikārātmanā svasaṃvedanena   
svānubhavena kriyādhikārātmanā yuktyā parameśvaraproktairāgamaiśca   
siddhaṃ maheśvararūpaṃ yat vitatyanirṇītaṃ tadeva saṃkṣepeṇa   
śiṣyabuddhiṣu niveśayituṃ saṃkṣipya sthāpayituṃ svātmaiva   
sarvajantūnā utpale nopapāditetyantena ślokāṣṭadaśakayukte nāhnike na   
tatvārthasaṃgrahaṃ paramārthabhūtārthasaṃgrahaṃ pradarśayati | tatra   
tatvārthasaṃgraharūpe āhnike śloke pāramārthikaṃ svarūpamuktvā   
patirevaṃ vidhastasya prameyamevaṃ vidhamiti mātṛmeya darśanadiśā   
ślokanavakena saṃsārātmakabandhasvarūpaṃ saptakena maheśvarātmaka   
svasvarūpapratyabhijñānātmakaṃ moṣatatvaṃ ślokena (tu)   
śuktārthopasaṃhāraṃ darśayati tātparyam |  
  
	sarvajantūnāmidamiti jaḍaparāmarśaviśrānti bhūtāhamiti   
parāmarśasvarūpāṇāṃ sarvajantūnāṃ madhyamā jīvābhāsā iti   
pūrvoktanītyā śivādisakalāntānāṃ pramātṝṇāṃ maheśvara eva   
svātmā teṣāṃ svātmaiva maheśvaraḥ sa caika eva deśakālākalita   
saṃvit svarūpatvād eka evā dvitīya eva | idantāmantarnītāṃ kṛtvā   
ahamityakhaṇḍāmarśabṛṃhitaḥ evaṃ rūpe svātmani svātantryeṇa   
vaiśvararūpapradarśanāt śivādikṣityanta viśvarūpaḥ |  
  
	ihetyavipratipattidyotakaṃ sarvasaṃpratipannamavyayam | ihāsmin   
jagati ghaṭapaṭādayo jaḍāstāvaccetana nimagnā eva bhānti |  
  
	cetananimagnatvena bhāvinamevadarśayati - idamiti jaḍaparāmarśaḥ   
| ahamiti saṃvitparāmarśa eva viśrāmyati | tena vinā tasyedamityasya   
vicchinna (ṭp. [385] 395) (497) iti nītyānyatra viśrāntya bhāvāt | tataśca   
tathā hi jaḍabhūtānāṃ ityuktanītyā jaḍānāmahamiti saṃvitparāmarśe   
viśrāntatvāt jaḍānāṃ nirātmatvāt jantavaḥ jīvā eva sātmānasteṣāṃ   
jantūnāṃ svātmaiva maheśvaraḥ sva svātmānatvanyaḥ kaścit svātmā   
saṃvitsvabhāva iti yataḥ atassvātmaiva maheśvaraḥ saṃvido   
deśakālākārairbhedo nāsti | vyāpāranityapūrṇasvarūpatvāt   
tairdeśādibhiratratyedānīṃ tana evamākāramityanyonyaṃ bhidyantām | te   
tu dehaprāṇabuddhyādayaḥ jaḍapakṣapatitāḥ jaḍavaccetana eva nimagna iti   
cidātmā eka eva deśakālākāraśūnyatvād ghaṭāderdehādeścaikatra   
svātmani vaiśvarūpyamābhāsayati iti yataḥ tataḥ vaiśvarūpyā   
bhāsanāt viśvātmikāmidantāmahantārūpaviśrāntāṃ   
kṛtvedantānunmukhasvātmamātraviśrāntirūpāhaṃ vimarśaparipūrṇaḥ   
ata eva śivādi sakalāntapramātṛvarganusyūtāhaṃ   
vimarśaparipūrṇatvād asya svātmanaḥ sarvajñatvasarvakartṛtve(te) nāsya   
yatnopapādye śrotāsmi spraṣṭāsmi rasayitāsmi ghrātāsmi   
jñānendriyasya vaktāsmi ādātāsmi gantāsmi visarjayitāsmi iti   
vicitrabuddhikarmendriya viṣaye jñātṛkartṛtve yathā ekasyaivātmanaḥ saṃ   
bhavataḥ parameśvare indriyakalpabhūtarudrakṣetrasahasraviṣayasya   
bhāvarāśisaṃbandhijñānaṃ kriyā ca rudrāḥ māyotīrṇāḥ   
pramātāraḥ sadgurukaṭākṣānugṛhītāśca rudrāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ   
māyāntarvartinaḥ pramātārasteṣāṃ tat tajjñānaṃ karaṇaṃ caikatra   
cidātmanyekasyaiva saṃbandhi bhavati | eka eva cidātmā rudrakṣetrajña   
pramātṛvargātmanā sthitvā jānāmi karomītyarthaḥ |  
  
	(498) svātmāmaheśvara(rūpa)ekaścet ghaṭādi dehādi viśrānti   
bhūmitvāt maheśvararūpasvātmā eka evā dvitīyaścet sthūlo'haṃ   
kṛśo'haṃ caitro'haṃ maitro'haṃ puṇyabhāgahaṃ   
pāpakarmāhamityādirātmano nānātvahetu bandhakaḥ   
tadbaṃdhasyāśrayaḥ kaḥ maheśvararūpasyātmano bandhā bhāvāt   
tadvyatiriktasyānyasya kasyāpyabhāvāt yasya saṃbandhasya avamocanāya   
vimokṣāya pratyabhijñāśāstropadeśaḥ |  
  
	(ṭp. [386] 396) tripratyayamidaṃ jñānaṃ gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ   
|  
  
	ityuktanītyā prathamaṃ gurupadeśaḥ tanmukhāt śāstrābhyāsaḥ   
tatassvānubhavaḥ ityādirūpaḥ |  
  
	ayamudyamaḥ yasya saṃbandhasyā va mocanāya |  
	tat prasādavaśād deva gurvāgamata eva vā ||  
śāstrād vā parameśasya yasmāttasmādupāyataḥ ||   
  
etat tatvaparijñānaṃ samokṣaḥ parameśatā |  
	tat pūrṇatvaṃ prabuddhānāṃ jīvanmuktiśca sā smṛtā || iti |  
  
evaṃ bhūte svātmani maheśvare sthite tasminneva prakāśarūpe   
svātmadarpaṇe svasṛṣṭe svātmanā parameśvareṇa sṛṣṭe bhāgamadhye   
idantā rūpaṃ buddhiprāṇadehādi yat tad grāhakātmanā anena   
parameśvareṇāhaṃkāraparāmarśapadaṃ nītam | tasya buddhyāderbandha   
iti śeṣaḥ |  
  
	tatreti svātmaiva sarvajantūnāmityukta prakāreṇa svātmani   
maheśvare sthite ityeko'rthaḥ | kiñca prakāśasvarūpe   
viśvapratibiṃbanakṣame pūrṇāhantātmani svātmadarpaṇe tena   
maheśvareṇa svasvarūpasaṃkocātmaka śūnya purassara idaṃ bhāgaḥ   
(499) sṛṣṭaḥ | tanmadhye idaṃ bhāvamadhye, idantayā vedya   
buddhiprāṇadeharūpaṃ yat tat svasmādbhinnaṃ ghaṭādi vedyatāyai   
samucitabuddhyādiridaṃ bhāvābhibhavā prabhaviṣṇutvāt kṛta kena   
pūrṇāhaṃ bhāvenāhaṃ devadattaḥ ahaṃ caitra iti ca kāsti |  
  
	evamastu buddhyādidyahaṃkāraparāmarśapadaṃ nītaṃ bhavatu |   
tathāpi kasya bandhaḥ īśvaravyatirikto'nyo nāsti buddhyādeḥ   
prakāśamānatveneśvarātmatvāt sa caitramaitrādi buddhyādirūpaḥ   
pramātā svarūpā parijñānamayaḥ pūrṇāhantā svarūpā parijñānena   
nirmitaḥ | ata eva tat tad dehaprāṇādigrahaṇenānekaḥ pumān   
bhoktāmataḥ puṇyapāpabhoktāmataḥ | tatra puṃsi īśvareṇa sṛṣṭau   
kriyānandau rajassatvaguṇaukrameṇa sukhaduḥkhātmako bhogaḥ   
ubhayorviśramasthānīyastamoguṇaḥ so'pi bhogarūpatvenamataḥ |   
satvarajastamomaya prakṛtimayatvāt tasya |  
  
	bhavaduktaṃ satyaṃ paramārthataḥ kaścin nasaṃbaṃdhaḥ   
saparameśvara eva sarvotkṛṣṭādati durghaṭakāriṇaḥ svātantryāt   
pūrṇāhantātmakaṃ svātmānaṃ saṃkucitabhavabhāsayati (ṭp. [387]   
397) yadā tadā bhāsanasamaye svasya pūrṇasya   
rūpasyābhāsamānatve'pyaparāmarśarūpamararijñānaṃ? yat   
tadaparijñānameva yasya caitrādeḥ puṃsaḥ kāraṇatvena kṛtam | satu   
śivo'hamīśvaro'hamityāderantaḥ sthitasyāpi pūrṇatvasyākhyāti   
mātrarūpaḥ puruṣa ucyate puruṣa ityucyamānatvādanekaḥ | anekatvameva   
pratipādayati tat tad iti | sthūlo'haṃ kṛśo'haṃ durbalo'haṃ prabalo'haṃ   
sukhyahaṃ duḥkhyahamiti tat tad dehaprāṇabuddhiviśeṣātmakasaṃkoca-   
svīkārādanekaḥ | ata eva pumān duḥkhasukhādibodharūpaṃ bandhamanu   
bhavati | bhogonāma tasya puṃsaḥ parameśvareṇa sṛṣṭau kalpitau   
kriyānandau | kalpitā kriyā hi duḥkhaṃ kriyāyāḥ rajorūpaṃ   
duḥakhatvaṃ darśayati - rajo'pi tyādinā | rajo hi satvatamasoḥ prakāśā   
prakāśayoḥ satvatamasoścāñcalyarūpaikadeśātmakamasthirarūpaṃ   
sukhamucyate | kevalaṃ prakāśasvarūpaṃ ca satvaṃ sukham |   
ubhayorapyaprakāśarūpa duḥkhasukhayoraprakāśarūpaḥ dvayoḥ   
pralayasthānīyaḥ | pralayasthānakalpanāmāha - tatra sṛṣṭau kriyānandā   
vityatra | sṛṣṭā vityanenā sṛṣṭamapi kimapyastīti sūcitam |  
  
	tayormadhye kiṃ vyavacchedyaṃ kiñca grāhyamityāśaṃkyāha -   
patyurdharaṇyādi śivānteṣu ahamityevaṃ parāmarśamayasya   
śivabhaṭṭārakasya te ṣvahamevati yajjñānaṃ teṣu tajjñānaprāṇana   
vimarśarūpā kriyā ca yāte ahamidamidamahamiti parāmarśarūpayoḥ   
sadāśiveśvarabhaṭṭārakayostadadhiṣṭheyayormantramaheśvarākhya   
pramātṛvargayoḥ krameṇasvātmabhūteṣu svāṅgabhūteṣu bhāveṣu   
māyāpramātu yadvanmūrdhādi pādāntaṃ svātmarūpabhūtaṃ tadvat   
svāṅgabhūteṣu bhāveṣu svāṅgabhūtatve na yat jñānamabodhaḥ   
svāṅgabhūtenāvamarśanaṃ kriyā te śivabhaṭṭārakasya jñānakriye   
sadāśiveśvarabhaṭṭārakayor-adhiṣṭhātṛ-  
rūpayoścāhamidamidamahamiti idantā prathamāṅkurasphuraṇāt te   
jñānakriye māyayā sahite bhavati | tatra yaṃ paśoḥ krameṇajñānaṃ   
satvaṃ kriyā rajaḥ māyātmataśceti bhavati | (501) viśvarūpasya   
śivabhaṭṭārakasya sadāśivādidharaṇyante sarvatrāhamiti yaḥ prakāśaḥ   
ahamiti tat prakāśānuprāṇakoyaśca vimarśaḥ te tāvat tasya (ṭp. 388)   
śivabhaṭṭārakasya jñānakriye anantaramahamiti   
svarūpaparāmarśamatyaktvaivāhamidamidamahamiti itīdantāṃ kuratā   
prathanarūpaṃ punarapyahamiti svarūpaparāmarśaviśrāntam |   
ahamidamidamahamiti sadāśiveśvaratā parāmarśaparamārthaṃ   
yadvimarśanaṃ idantāṅkurapradhānatvāt sadāśiveśvarabhaṭṭārakaḥ   
yena śivabhaṭṭārakeṇa nirmitā sadāśiveśvarabhaṭṭāraka saṃbandhinī   
sā māyāśaktiḥ jñānakriyā māyātmikāstisraḥ śaktayaḥ bhagavati   
sadāśivabhaṭṭārake īśvarabhaṭṭārake ca krameṇāsṛṣṭāḥ naisargikyaḥ   
svata eva siddhāḥ tasyaiva bhagavataḥ svamāyāśaktyā gūhita   
svarūpatvāt svasvarūpāparijñāne sati svāṅgabhūteṣvapi   
svasvarūpādanyonyataśca bhinneṣu bhāveṣu ahamahamevedamidameveti   
yajjñānaṃ sukharūpaṃ satvaṃ tad bhinnabhāvasaṃbandhinī kriyā rajaḥ   
duḥkhaṃ tadubhaya prakāśavimarśaśūnyaṃ māyārūpaṃ tamo mohaḥ   
paśoḥ prakāśajñānarūpaṃ satvaṃ sukhaṃ prakāśā prakāśau   
rajorūpaṃ duḥkhamubhayoraprakāśastamo rūpo moha iti krameṇa   
jñānakriyā māyā paśoḥ satvarajastamāṃsi bhavanti |  
  
	jñānakriyā māyā eva krameṇa satvarajastamāṃsi cetatāḥ   
jñānakriyāmāyā parameśvarasya yathā avyatirekiṇyaḥ śaktaya   
ityucyante tadvatpaśoḥ satvarajastamāṃsi avyatirekiṇyaḥ śaktaya iti   
prasajyante | tāni sukhaduḥkhamoharūpatayā bhogyatvājjaḍāni tāni   
cidrūpāt pustatvād vyatiriktāni bhaṇyante | (502) tadetat kathamiti   
saṃśayaṃ rāmayitumāha - ahaṅkārādyupasthāntaḥkaraṇatvena   
śabdādi prṭhivyantakāryatvena pariṇāmināmeṣāṃ satvarajastamasāṃ   
guṇānāṃ paśoraśaktimatve'pi bhavatāśaktimatvenāśaṃkyamānatvāt   
bheda sthiteḥ bhedena sthitatvā cchaktitvaṃ nāpadiśyate   
guṇatvamevāpadiśyata ityarthaḥ |  
  
	yad bhavaduktaṃ tat satyamityākṣepoktiḥ | evamiti |   
satvarajastamasāmapi śaktitvaṃ syāt | teṣāṃ puruṣeṇa sahabhedagraho   
yadi na bhavet idānīṃ satvarajastamasāṃ puruṣeṇāyaṃ bheda vyavahāro   
vicāryate | atra ca bhedavyavahāre puruṣaḥ saṃkucitacinmātrasvabhāvaḥ   
asya puruṣasya ghaṭapaṭādi bhāvaviṣayaḥ prakāśavimarśanarūpaṃ (ṭp.   
389) na naisargikam sahajam | asya paśoḥ sahajaṃ cet   
suṣuptādyavasthāyāmapi prakāśanādi prasaṅgāt | anya saṃbandha   
kṛtaṃ parameśvarasaṃbandha kṛtaṃ, tataśca naisargikatvābhāvād   
aśaktimatve'pi śaktimatvena śaṃkyamānāt paśoḥ bhede na yataḥ etāni   
satvādīni sthitāni tada bhedena sthitatvād vyatirekamuktāśśaktayaḥ iti   
nocyante | vyatiriktānyeva paśorūpakaraṇatvāt   
sukhaduḥkhamohātmakabhogyopakaraṇarūpatvāt guṇā ityucyante |   
satvādayaḥ puruṣāt kimiti bhede neṣyante | ucyate - bhede naiveṣyante   
abhedeneṣyate ced vakṣyamāṇo doṣo bhavati | sukhaduḥkhamohātmaka   
raṇamayo daśakaṃ sukhaduḥkhamohapariṇāmaṃ rūpaṃ kāryadaśakaṃ   
ca tat pariṇāmamayatvāt sukhaduḥkhamohasvabhāvatvenānubhūyata iti   
karaṇakāryavargatādātmyavṛttayaḥ sukhaduḥkhamohāḥ karaṇakārya-----  
-------- janavat puruṣasthāpi tādātmyaṃ bhajeran yadi tarhi puruṣa eva   
kāryaparyantakaraṇaparyantaḥ sṛṣṭimayaḥ (503) sampannaḥ bījāṃkurādi   
vat pariṇāme cetanasya na yujyate, parasparasvabhāvatva ityādinā   
ślokatrayeṇa pariṇāmaśca dūṣitaḥ | svātantryaśaktyabhāve'pi puruṣo   
viśvarūpa ityāyātam | prakṛtyādi kṣitiparyanta viśvarūpa ityāyātam |   
tathā svātantryaśaktyā viśvarūpatve puruṣo na kaścid asti | asya puruṣatva   
meva na bhavati | īśvaratvameva bhavati | uktametat sarvaṃ   
prasaṅgāpādanam | tasmāt prasaṃgā pādanatvāt   
svasvarūpāparijñānamayo naikaḥ pumān mata ityuktanītyā   
apratyabhijñānamayapuruṣasvarūpavicāre satvādayo guṇāḥ   
puruṣadbhinna eveti sthitam |  
  
	jñānakriyāmāyāḥ paśuṃ pratikathaṃ satvādi rūpā guṇā   
bhavantītyante vāsi praśnamāśaṃkyāha - jñānakriyāmāyānāṃ   
paśuṃ pratiguṇī bhāvamevāha - sṛṣṭyādinā viśvapālayituḥ patyuḥ   
sattā viśvabhavanakartṛtvaṃ saivakriyā vimarśātmacamatkāravyatirekāt   
saiva sattānandapareṇamukhyatyāgena svātmaviśrāntirūpatvāt paśostad   
bhāvaḥ | evaṃ bhūsattānandayorabhāva eva paśuṃ pratimohātmā tamo   
guṇo bhavati | satvaguṇātmikā sukhaduḥkharūpā etayoraṃśena sadbhāva   
eva sukharūpaṃ satvaṃ paśorasti satvarajasorātmā miśrasvabhāvo yaḥ   
anyonyaśleśisatvatamomayaṃ (ṭp. 390) tad duḥkharūpaṃ rajaḥ   
patyurjñānaśaktiḥ patyuḥ paśvavasthāyāṃ satvaṃ rajaḥ kriyāśaktiḥ   
māyāśaktistamaḥ |  
  
	ihāsmin saṃviddarśane viśvasya prakāśanāvaicitryalakṣaṇena   
sṛṣṭyādi nāpañcakṛtyena pālayitā svayaṃ prakāśasvabhāvaḥ   
patirityucyate sā sphurattā mahāsattetyatra pūrvavyākhyātā tasya   
viśvapateḥ bhavana kartṛtā sattā svātmano viśvātmanā bhavana krtṛtā   
yā sā sattaiva svabhāvamavabhāsasyetyuktanītyā (504) prakāśasya   
viśvabhavanakartṛtā svātantrya svaparameśvarasya prāṇabhūtavimarśā   
vyatirekādvimarśaḥ so'hamityuktanītyā ahamiti   
vimarśātmakākārarūpā satī kriyāśaktirucyate | viśvaprakāśanātmikā   
sattaiva kriyāśaktirityucyate | viśvapateḥ sā sattaiva   
svavyatiriktavastvanatarā bhāvāt paraunmukhyatyāgena   
svātmaviśrāntirūpa ānando bhavati | bhagavataścidātmataive yad rūpā   
sattārūpā | ānandarūpā kriyārūpā ca | paśostvaṃśena satā   
ānandaścobhayorabhāvaśca bhavati | saṃkucitacidrūpatvāt   
sattānandayorabhavatā | tane saṃkucita cidrūpatvena paśuṃ prati yaḥ   
sattānandayoraṃśaḥ paśoḥ prakāśasukhavṛttisatvam | tatra sattāyāḥ   
aṃśaḥ prakāśavṛttiḥ | etad ubhayātmakaṃ satvaṃ sattānandayorabhāvo   
yaḥ tat krameṇa āvaraṇamoharūpaṃ tamaḥ prakāśasyābhāva   
āvaraṇarūpaṃ tamaḥ ānandasyābhāvamoharūpaṃ tamaḥ te ete   
satvatamasī  yathā nīlātmakamanīlātmakaṃ ca vastu yathā   
prasparaparihāreṇa vartate tadvat parasparaparihāreṇa kāryakāraṇatvavat   
vartete yadyapi tathāpyekasya pramātuḥ satvarajasoḥ saṃbandhina ekena   
parāmarśena ----- kāryadharmyapekṣayā citragatapataṅga   
dharmigatanīlātmakarūpanyāyodharmiḥ pramātā tasyāpekṣayā   
vibhātaḥ | ataḥ miśratayā bhāvanāt dvayasyātmā   
satvatamasormiśrasvabhāvatvāt | atra rajoguṇaprakāśā prakāśarūpayoḥ   
satvatamasoḥ śleṣeṇāva sthānamiti duḥkhatvam | priyataputrādeḥ   
tadekaghanaḥ nīrogonirūpadrava bahiḥ prakāśaḥ sukham | ekaghanaḥ   
apunardarśanarūpaḥ aprakāśomohaḥ yastu kathaṃ cit prakāśaḥ ahitayā   
pratyakṣeṇa dṛśyamānayā savyādhikadeharūpatayā yastu (ṭp. 391)   
kathaṃ cit prakāśaḥ pramātrāderiṣṭayā abhimatayā gatagadādayaḥ   
kalyāṇādharmayogitāyāḥ kathañcidaprakāśaḥ tadeva rogasya   
prakāśaḥ nīrogatāyāḥ aprakāśa ityubhayamapi duḥkhatatvaṃ pūrvatā   
paramārthaṃ rogasya prakāśaḥ paścād bhāvinyā nīrogatāyāḥ   
prakāśa iti rogasya pūrvāparībhāvasāraḥ kriyā yāḥ paramārthaḥ |   
anena prakāśarūpaḥ satvaṃ, aprakāśarūpaṃ tamaḥ   
prakāśāprakāśarūpaṃ rajaścoktam | rajaḥ satvatamasorubhayātmakaṃ   
bhavatu | ubhayoranubhayābhāvātmakaḥ paśoścaturtho guṇo nāsti |   
kathamiti cet tasyānubhayarūpasya guṇasya kalpitākalpitarūpāyāḥ   
aniścayā niścayarūpāyāṃ pramātuḥ pratītau dhiyi ananupraveśāt tasya   
| tathā hi ananupraveśameva dyotayati - idaṃ nīlamiti | pramāturniścitāyā   
dhiyibhāti nīlābhāvaḥ anīlātmako nīlābhāvastu nīlaprakāśakāle   
nīlapadaprakāśamānatvād vikalpakalpitaḥ | etan nīlapratiyogī kaścidastīti   
bhāsamānatvād vyavahāraparamārthaḥ nīlasyā nīlasya ca pratyakṣasya   
cāpratyakṣasyā nīlasya cetyubhayavyāmiśraṇāt tu nīlānīlaṃ   
nāmavastubhātussatvatamasorabhāvātmakamanubhayarūpaṃ yad vastu   
tadakalpita yā pratyakṣībhūta yā nīlapratīti nyāyena na viṣayī kṛtaṃ   
caitadanubhayarūpaṃ vastu akalpitā anīladhiyamanudhāvet |   
pratyakṣānnīladhiyaṃ praviśati cet tarhi kalpitāmanīladhiyamanudhāvet |   
svata eva vastutvā bhāvādakalpitāṃ nīladhiyaṃ na praviśati | ata eva   
kalpitamanīladhiyañca nānudhāvati vastu |  
  
	ākṣipati - atheti | tadanubhayātmakaṃ vastu kalpitāmanīladhiyaṃ   
(506) nāviśatīti cet | akalpitayā pratyakṣabhūtayā nīladhiyā viṣayī   
kṛtaṃ nīlamevasyāt | tadanubhayamakalpitaviṣayī kṛtaṃ nīlasamānaṃ   
satvameva syāt | na paśoścaturtho'sti guṇassūtragataḥ | apiśabdaścārthe |   
paśoḥ sā viśvapateḥ sattā paśoḥ satvaṃ tadabhāvastamaḥ dvayātmā   
raja iti saṃbaṃdhaḥ ||  
  
	eva muktaprakāreṇapatirūpaṃ paśurūpaṃ pramātṛtattvaṃ ca   
nirṇītam | (ṭp. 392) patyuḥ paśośca prameyatatvaṃ nirṇetuṃ prathamaṃ   
patyā vitthaṃ vakṣyamāṇarūpaṃ prameyatattvaṃ nirṇetu māha - ye   
bhāvāḥ prabhorayaṃ ghaṭaḥ ayaṃ paṭa iti sāṅketika   
vyavahārarahitatvād asāmayikedantā sāṅketikedantā   
parāmarśagocarāḥ ke vibhāvāḥ miśrāmiśrarūpatayā paśoryathā   
prabhorapi miśrāmiśrarūpatayā citrāvabhāsinaḥ aneka   
sāmānyasamudāyātmaka svalakṣaṇarūpāḥ vibhinnāḥ anyonya   
vyāmiśraṇaśūnyāḥ sāmānyātmanaḥ bhāvā bhāsante |  
  
	ihāsmin saṃviddarśane idametādṛgityādi ṣvābhāsā evārthā   
ityuktam | te cārthāḥ śukloghaṭa ityādi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyarūpeṇa kadācin   
miśrī kriyate yadā padārthānāṃ svalakṣaṇarūpatā kadācid   
ekādhikaraṇā viśrāntāḥ pṛthak pṛthageva parāmṛśyante yadā   
sāmānyarūpatā sāmānya viśeṣarūpatve nobhayātmano'rthāḥ   
asāmayikenāyaṃ ghaṭaḥ ayaṃ paṭa ityakalpitena   
sahajabhedaparāmarśarūpeṇa svābhāvikabheda   
parāmarśarūpeṇāṅgulī nirdeśādi prakhye nedaṃ bhāvena gocarī   
kāryāḥ prabhorapi na kevalaṃ sadyojātasya tadānīṃ jātasya   
nālasyāvyutpannasya cānucitasāṅketika vyavahārasya sāmayikedantā   
parāmarśabhuvo bhūtvā sāmānya viśeṣātmanā citragatayā va bhāsate   
prabhorapi neśvarasyā (507) vicitratayā va bhāsam | citratvaṃ nāma   
svalakṣaṇātmakamiśratvaṃ ca bhittitala iva yugapadekāhantā   
viśrāntatayā bhānam | īśvaradaśāyāḥ viśvollāsanāntarīyakatvena   
avinābhāvatvena pūrṇāhantātmaka saṃvitsaṃkocarūpa saṃvitpramāṇe   
naiva prakāśamānaṃ, niṣedhyavastūparakto hi na arthaḥ |   
atreśvaradaśāyāṃ śūnyamidamaṃśollāsādahamaṃśasya   
kiñcinniṣedhyarūpaṃ śūnyam | ahantāniṣedharūpā   
sāmayikīmidantāmullāsayati | evaṃ tāvadīśvarasya |  
  
	itthaṃ prameyatatvaṃ bhagavati paramaśive prameyakathaina na   
bhavati bhagavataḥ prameya kathotthāpakatvameva sadāśiveśvaratvam |   
  
	patyau prameyavṛttāntaṃ nirupya paśuṃ pratiprameyavṛttāntaṃ   
nirūpayati ślokatrayeṇa | ye turviśeṣaṃ dyotayati | paśoritthaṃ bhūtaṃ   
prameyaṃ na tvīśvaravaduktanyāyena (ṭp. 393) miśratayā   
bhidyamānāvabhāsā arthāḥ svalakṣaṇarūpāḥ sāmānyarūpāśca te   
pratyagātmanastu smṛtyutprekṣādi gocare smṛtā butprekṣāyāmanubhave   
vikalpe saṅkalpādau priyo'yaṃ śatrurayamityādyābhiranyonya-   
bhinnābhiḥ saṃjñābhiḥ prakalpyāḥ vikalpanīyāḥ bhāvānāṃ   
viśeṣānusāreṇa tatatsukhaduḥkhādi kāraṇībhiḥ saṃjñābhiḥ   
prakalpyāḥ | tasya paśoḥ priyo'yaṃ śatrurayamityasādhāraṇī mama   
śatrurmama mitramiti pratipramātṛniyatā sṛṣṭiḥ īśasṛṣṭaḥ mama caitraḥ   
mamamaitra ityādi vastūpajīvanī saiṣāsṛṣṭiḥ, tadātmanaḥ   
īśvarātmanaḥ paśoḥ | pūrṇāhantātmaka svātmaviśrāntyuparodhāya ca   
layaspandamānayā tat tadākārādivarṇavaicitryacitrayā brahmyādi devatā   
cakramayyā prāṇarūpayā prāṇātmikayā (508) paśoḥ jñānatvena   
vartamāna yeśvaraśaktyotthāpitayā tat tad varṇavaicitryucitayā priyaḥ   
śatrurityādi tat tad varṇavaicitrya citrayā vikalpaśaktyā tasya   
paśorasādhāraṇī sṛṣṭiḥ |  
  
	īśvaravargāt paśusṛṣṭerviśeṣaṃ dyotayati ------------ tadevāha   
pratyagātmanaḥ paśorarthāḥ vakṣyamāṇarūpeṇārthāḥ   
prameyarūpāḥ īśvarasya yathā ----------------  
  
atra granthapāta iva   
  
(509) arthāḥ asāmayikedantā parāmarśabhuvaḥ tathā na sāmayikedantā   
parāmarśabhuva eva bhavanti | miśratayeti svalakṣaṇātmanā   
sāmānyātmanā ca bhidyamānaḥ prakāśo yeṣāṃ te   
viśeṣasāmānyātmāno'rthāḥ prati puruṣaṃ bhinnabhinnatvenāñcati   
viśrāmyatīti pratyagātmā asaṃkīrṇāhaṃ prakāśātmā   
aṣṭāratnimātre deha eva sthito yasyā hantā tasya vikalpanīyāḥ   
patyuravikalpanīyāḥ pratiprāṇi pratipuruṣaṃ tat tad   
anubhavavāsanānusāreṇa priyo'yaṃ śatrurayamityādibhirvibhinnābhiḥ   
priyo'yaṃ śatrurayamiti priyatva śatrutva bhāvanāviśeṣānusāreṇa   
krameṇa tat tad vicitrasukhaduḥkhādyupayuktibhiḥ saṃjñābhiḥ smaraṇe   
utprekṣaṇe saṅkalpe pratyakṣapṛṣṭhapātini vikalpe anusaṃdhāne   
vikalpanīyā iti saṃbaṃdhaḥ |   
  
	(ṭp. 394)  atra tātparyārthamāha - īśvarasya proyo'yaṃ   
śatrurayamityādi vikalpātmatāmantareṇārthāḥ ahamidamidamahamiti   
śuddhavimarśaviṣayī bhāvyā arthāḥ paśo'stute arthāḥ anyonyāpohane   
kautukinivikalpe samārūḍhā bhavanti | saṃsārabaṃdhinaḥ śatrorhānaṃ   
mitrasya dānamityādi heyopādeyādivyavahāropayogāt te arthāḥ vikalpe   
samāruḍhā eva bhānti | patyuravikalpatve yāvāne vārthaḥ   
paśostāvāneva | tat tasmāt prameyasya patirūpatāyāṃ ko viśeṣaḥ |   
tasyeti paśoḥ paśukartṛkā sṛṣṭiḥ īśvarasṛṣṭānāmuparivartinī | atra eva   
kāmīśvarasṛṣṭimupajīvantī asādhāraṇīti pratipramātṛniyatā   
kumbhakārasṛṣṭiḥ | anyā tu tunnakārasṛṣṭiranyetyādi   
pratipramātṛniyatā | tadeva pratipādayati - tadyatheti idaṃ hṛdyamiti |   
yadvastu yena sṛṣṭaṃ tat tasyaiva tathā śleṣmiṇa ikṣurneṣṭaḥ kuṣṭhinaḥ   
(510) rāṅkavaṃ puruṣamiti tat tasyaiva hṛdyaṃ nānyasya īśvaravat   
paśorapi sṛṣṭiśaktirasti | tarhi paśuvat īśvara eva | satyam | asāvapīśvaraḥ   
paśusṛṣṭerapīśvara sṛṣṭiḥ pṛthivyādivat paśorapi sṛṣṭiḥ   
sarvasādhāraṇī kathaṃ na bhavati | ahamapīśvaraḥ īśvaraśaktyāhaṃ   
sṛjāmīti parijānīyāt yadi sādhāraṇī bhavet yāvatā tathā naḥ sā   
svaśaktiḥ tasyā parijñātā svaśaktiṃ na jānāti | paravaśasyeva tasyā   
satastasyāsauśatruretanmitramiti vikalpaśaktirudeti | sā vikalpanaśaktiḥ   
kenāvāpyate |  
  
	pariharati - aheti | pūrṇāhaṃ parāmarśarūpatayā   
śabdarāśilakṣaṇasyeśvarasyāhaṃ svarūpaviśrāntalakṣaṇāyāḥ   
parameśvaratāyā uparodhaprayojanā brahmādi devatā cakramayī   
taistairākārādi varṇavaicitryai vicitrā yā śaktistayā śaktyotthāpita -------  
rasau paśorvikalpakriyā ekasminnapi vastunyasthairyājjalacandravaccañcalā   
cañcalatvāt mitraṃ śatruriti varṇavaicitryānubaddhā tayā   
vikalpanakriyayā tadātmana īśvarasvabhāvasyaiva paśoḥ   
paśorasādhāraṇī sṛṣṭiḥ pañcadantaścaturvaktrohastī nabhāsidhāvatī   
(ṭp. 395) pañcasaṃkhyā hastinaḥ paśukalpitāyāṃ miśratāyāmapi   
vikalpasṛṣṭiḥ tānīśvarasṛṣṭān pañcasaṃkhyādyā   
bhāsānevopajīvatīti sarvāpāśavīvikalpasṛṣṭirīśvarasṛṣṭyupajīvanīti   
uktam |  
  
	uktaprakāreṇa pāśavī kartṛtā sṛṣṭiḥ paśoḥ saṃsārarūpā tarhi   
parameśvarakartṛkā sṛṣṭiḥ paśoḥ kiṃ kuryāt | aiśaḥ sargaḥ dvidhā   
sādhāraṇaḥ anyathā ca spaṣṭā va bhāsavān sādhāraṇo ghaṭādiḥ   
anyathetyasādhāraṇodvicaṃdrādiḥ | (511) kiñcānyatheti parijñātasya   
śaktitaḥ parijñāteśvara tādātmyaścet paśorapi sṛṣṭiḥ sādhāraṇī   
bhavati | ubhayātmāpi sargaḥ anyonyā pohanavikalpahā nenāhamidamiti   
sadā śivavat aikāgryāt krameṇāhamidamitīśvaratā padaṃ paśorapi   
bhavati |  
  
	anyatheti padena nirdiṣṭo dvicandrādi rubhayasya sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ   
ghaṭādeva ghaṭādirūpeṇa prakāśanaṃ dvicandrāderdvicandrādirūpeṇa   
prakāśanam | ubhayātmāpi sargaḥ ahamapyanyaścaitraḥ anyo   
ghaṭādiranya ityevaṃ bhūtavikalpahānakrameṇāhamevedamiti nirvikalpena   
parigṛhītena spṛṣṭāme arthe ubhayātmanyarthe ahamevedamityekāgra   
parāmarśamavalaṃ nyāhamidameveti paśoryadā   
aiśvaraparāmarśapadaṃ bhavati puraḥ sthitasya vastuno'ntarhṛdaye   
lagnatvamasmin nimeṣonmeṣarahitā   
bahirdṛṣṭirityādyupadeśakrameṇābhyāsātiśayena paśoḥ paśutvaṃ   
pratihanti aiśvarī sṛṣṭirīśvaratvaṃ ca darśayati |  
  
	kiñca tasyā sādhāraṇītyādi ślokena yo'yaṃ vikalpaḥ sargaḥ |   
aparijñātasvaśaktikasya aparijñāteśvaratādātmyasya   
paśoryo'sādhāraṇaḥ sarga utkaḥ | anyatheti | tad viparītenāparijñāta yā   
īśvaraśaktyā parijñātatādātmyasya bhavati yadā tadā paśoḥ sargaḥ   
sādhāraṇa eva āpyāyanamabhiṣekā dineṣṭapoṣaṇam | abhicāraṇaṃ   
śatruvargasya hiṃsārogaśāntyādi nyastamantrabhavitāntaḥ karaṇasya   
sādhakasyāpyāyanābhicaraṇādiryathā sarvasādhāraṇo bhavati tadvat   
paśorapi sargaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ |  
  
	evamuktaprakāreṇānyonyāpohanātmakavikalpatyāgena   
nirvikalpakarūpātmī bhāve (ṭp. 396) viśvasyāhamidamidamahamityahantā   
sātkāralakṣaṇaḥ svapratyayaḥ (512) paśoḥ svānubhavasiddhaḥ mokṣo   
darśita iti vikalpahāne'nyetyanye | adhunā vikalpahānyabhāve'pi   
tanmokṣaṃ darśayati - śivādikṣityantaḥ ayaṃ tatvagrāmaḥ   
sarvomamāyaṃ vibhava ityevaṃ parijānataḥ ata eva viśvātmanaḥ   
paśorvikalpānāṃ prasāro'pi maheśatā bhavati |  
  
	pratyagātmeti | yo'haṃ pratipuruṣamavyāmiśrasva-  
saṃvedanānugamarūpaḥ anyaḥ kaścit paśuḥ nāhaṃ svāṅgarūpeṣu   
bhāveṣvityuktanītyā svātmāṅgatvena parigṛhīta   
grāhyagrāhakarūpāhaṃ prakāśaghanaḥ parameśvaraḥ ahaṃ sa eva   
so'pyahameva na tvanyaḥ | atadvyatirikto na bhavati | ata āvayoranyonya   
vyatirekā bhāvāt ghaṭapaṭādisaṃbandhinī vikalpasṛṣṭirapi   
svātantryalakṣaṇo mama vibhavaḥ | evaṃ bhūtavimarśe dṛḍhībhūte sati   
aparikṣīṇavikalpo'pi jīvanneva muktaḥ ahamanyaḥ parameśvaro'pyanyaḥ   
ghaṭādirapyanyaḥ ityevaṃ bhūtāṃ saṃsārahetu bhūtāṃ śaṅkāmapi   
naśaṅketa | idaṃ parameśvarātmakamātmasvarūpaṃ niśśaṅkatvena   
sphuṭaṃ yathoktaṃ vikalpo hi nāma na mūrchā prāyaṃ tato   
vikalpamānamapi prakāśa iti sthite prakāśamānatvādeva brahmavat   
satyameveti |   
  
	baddhamuktaḥ prameyaṃ prati ko bhedaḥ muktaḥ parameśvara iva   
meyaṃ svātmā bhedena sādhāraṇaṃ manyate | baddhaḥ   
punarmeyamatyantamabhedaṃ manyate | śrīmatsadāśiveśvara-  
paryantādārabhya kṛmiparyantaṃ pramātṛvargādhiṣṭhātṛ ahamiti   
yadrūpaṃ tadevātmatayābhiniviśate | yathoktam -  
  
	pratyekaṃ pratibhāti yadvaṣududayaṃ māṃ pratyudetītyayaṃ   
	mārtāṇḍo bhagavān mahīdharapuragrāmā ṭavīvartinām |  
	pṛthvīpūrva sadāśivāntapadavī sañcāriṇāṃ prāṇināṃ   
	pratyekaṃ pratibhāti tadvadahamityeka pramātā śivaḥ || iti |  
  
	tataścābhinaveśād viśvasya pramātṛvargasya yat prameyaṃ   
tanmamāpi prameyaṃ viśvapramātṛmayatvān mama prameyaṃ yat tad   
viśvasyāpi prameyam | ghaṭapaṭādiprameyaṃ ca prameyāntaradehādi ca   
mamaivāṅgabhūtam |  
  
(p. 397) aṅgabhūtatvameva darśayati - parasparataśca   
prameyavargācca | vyāvṛttaṃ sarvaṃ prameyamekarasābheda viśrānti   
paramārtham ahamiti parāmarśapadamupaiti | baddhasya tu sarvametat   
prameyaṃ prameyād bhinnaṃ pramātṛvargāccābhinnamiti śuddhabhedaika   
viśrāntabaddhaḥ |  
  
	svāṅgarūpeṣvityādinā ye'pya sāmayikedantetyādinā ca   
sadāśiveśvarabhuvimeyaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ mukta iti | jīvanmukta-  
padebaddhaḥ punarapyantabhedavat | ityanena baddharūpa paśumātṛviṣaye   
ca prameya vṛttāntaḥ parīkṣitaḥ | paramaśivetvasau prameya vṛttāntaḥ   
kathamityāśaṃkyāha - sarvathā prameya prakāreṇa pramātṛprakāreṇa   
cāntarālīnānantatatvādhanirbharaḥ cidānandaghanaḥ   
paramākṣaravigrahaḥ paramaśivaḥ antarālīnaḥ pūrṇāhantātmani   
svarūpe āsamantāllīnaḥ śivādikṣityantānantatvaughatvaudha   
nirbharācinmayānandaghanopadeśyākṣarasvarūpākārādi kṣakārānta   
pañcāśadakṣaravācaka śivādikṣityanta ṣaṭtriṃśat tatvātmaka vācya   
kāraṇabhūtaparamākṣaravigrahaḥ |  
  
	pūrṇāhantārūpā paramaśive prameya kathākācinnāsti | tatra hetu   
māha - śivādikṣityanta tatvaughasya tatra paramaśive sarvaprakāreṇa   
prameyarūpeṇa pramātṛrūpeṇa ca cidrūpatāmātraviśrāntatve   
vilīnatvāt | tataśca vilīnatvāt sā paramaśivasyāvasthā   
pūrṇāhantātmakabodhasvabhāvena dehādikāluṣyarahitatvādakṛtrimeṇa   
ata eva naisargikeṇa ata eva svābhāvikena sahajenāhamiti   
svātmacamatkāralakṣaṇena nānandenaikaghanā aparicchinna   
tādṛgvidhānandarūpā uktena paramākṣareṇa vigrahavatī śivādikṣityanta   
viśvottīrṇasya śivādikṣityanta viśvamayasya pade   
jyotiranuttaramityuktanītyānuttarajyotīrūpasya galitaprameyakathā   
sarvottīrṇā avasthā vyapadiśyate |  
  
	jñānādhikāra kriyādhikārāgamādhikāra   
tatvārthasaṃgraharūpādhikāra catuṣṭayātmaka   
śrīmadīśvarapratyabhijñāśāstroktaṃ yadvastu pratipāditaṃ   
prameyametacchāstraparāmarśaphalasya tat phalamāha |  
  
	ukta prakāreṇātmānamīśvararūpametasyātmanaḥ   
saṃbandhinyautada (ṭp. 398) viyukte tayā prāṇabhūte jñānakriye paśyan   
eva mīśvararūpo'yaṃ mamātmā tasya vyatirikte jñānakriye iti   
sākṣātkāreṇanubhavan sākṣātkurvan yathepsitā niṣṭānarthān jānāti   
karoti ca |  
  
	ātmānamīśvararūpaṃ tasya ca svāvyatirikte īśvararūpatā   
pratyabhijñānahetu bhūte jñānakriye jānan evaṃ bhūtaḥ   
paramaśivarūpo mamātmāna tu vai śeṣikanaiyāyikādibhirdarśitaḥ | tasya   
jñānakriye evaṃ bhūte na tu tasya vyatirikte sahaje (515) kecana ityevaṃ   
parāmṛśan yadyadicchati tat tat jānāti ca karoti ca muhūrtaṃ smarata   
ityādi krameṇa muhūrtayā māyāmadvayasamāveśābhyāsaparaḥ,   
anenaiva śarīreṇa jānāti ca karoti ceti saṃbandhaḥ | etat paraḥ evaṃ yo   
vedatatvena ityuktanītyā samāveśābhyāsarahitastu dehe satyāpi   
jīvanmuktaḥ jīvanneva śivaḥ dehapāte tu parameśvara eveti |  
  
	asya śāstrādhikāriṇaḥ svānubhava siddhasya   
śāstrārthasyopodbalakaḥ guruparamparārūpo vaktavya āgamādhikāreṇa   
śāstrasiddhānubhavo darśitaḥ | tripratyayamidaṃ jñānaṃ gurutaḥ   
śāstrataḥ svataḥ | ityetad dṛḍhīkṛtaṃ bhavati | ityābhiprāyeṇa   
gurupāramparyaṃ darśayati |  
  
	eṣa śāstramārgaḥ kathaṃcidāsādyetyādinā prakaṭitaḥ navaḥ   
sarvarahasyaśāstrāntargatatvāt gūḍhaḥ eṣaḥ śāstramārgaḥ yathā   
mahāgurubhiḥ śrīmat somānandadaiśikairmahāgurubhiḥ   
śivadṛṣṭiśāstre yathā sughaṭa ityucyate tat tasmād atra śāstramārge   
padaṃ parāmṛśan vidadhat viśrāmayat adhikārī ātmanaḥ śivatāmayīṃ   
bhuvanakartṛtāṃ vibhāvya jīvanmukto bhavati | evaṃ   
mārgamaniśamaviśaccharīraprāṇabuddhiśūnyāṃ tatraiva nimajya   
tameva mārgamaniśamāviśan siddhyati vibhūtīrlabhate |   
  
	asmat parameṣṭhinaḥ śrīmallakṣmaṇaguptācāryasyāsmat   
parameṣṭhinaḥ śrīmadutpaladevācāryabhaṭṭāraka   
śrīsomānandanāthapādāḥ tairukte śivadṛṣṭiśāstre abhinavaḥ   
sarvarahasya śāstrāntargataḥ sannigūḍhatvādaprasiddhaḥ bāhya caryā   
prāṇāyāmādyāsana bandhādiḥ | (516) ābhyantaracāryā dhyānādi |   
evaṃ bhūtabāhyāntaracaryā prāṇāyāma kleśaprayāsa kalāvirahāt   
sughaṭastāvaduktaḥ mārga evātra (p. 399) śrīmadīśvarapratyabhijñā   
śāstre paravādakalaṅkāpasāraṇenāvaraṇarūpabauddhādi   
paravādakalaṅkaśaṅkāpasāraṇe prakaṭatāṃ nītaḥ ayamarthaḥ   
śāstragurusvapratyaya siddha iti yataḥ tasmād atrāsmin śāstraprameye   
padaṃ parāmarśaṃ vidadhat viśramayan viśvakartṛtvalakṣaṇam   
aiśvaryamātmano vibhāvya śivādikṣityanta-viśvakartṛtvalakṣaṇam-  
aiśvaryaṃ vibhāvyabudhvā dārḍhye dṛḍhātmano niścaye   
pūrvamevāntassthitaṃ gurumukhena pratyabhijñāya parāmṛśati yadā   
tadā tadaiśvaryaparāmarśamātrād eva prathamaṃ jīvanmukto bhagavān   
śiva eva parameṣṭhipādaiḥ śrīsomānandadeśikaiḥ suvarṇe sakṛt jñāte   
idaṃ suvarṇamevaṃ bhūtametat pramāṇamiyadvarṇamiti jñāte suvarṇe   
punastat suvarṇaṃ pratikaraṇaṃ nikarṣaṇaṃ bhāvanā unmānaṃ ca mā   
vrajet | sakṛjjñātamātreṇedamiti dṛḍhaniścayatvāt dārḍhyaṃ   
svapitarisvabhūmyādau sakṛjjñāte punarjñāpakāpekṣā jñānāpekṣā   
ca na bhavati | pramāṇena svapratyayena śāstrād vā guruvākyato vā   
sarvastha ātmanaḥ śivatve dṛḍhātmanaḥ pratipattyā jñāte karaṇe   
nāsanabandhanādinā bhāvanā yāmasyā bhavanayāpi vā ayaṃ pitā   
ayaṃ bhrātā iti dārḍhye nātmanaḥ śivatvasya satyatā bhavati |   
śivatāmayīmātmano viśvakartṛtāmavabudhya niścitya muhūrtādi   
krameṇa yadyaniśamāviśati |  
  
	āveśameva darśayati - śarīraprāṇabudhiśūnyeṣu madhye   
abhyaṃtara dehamekaṃ vā dvayaṃ dehaṃ ca prāṇaṃ ca vā trayaṃ   
dehaṃ prāṇaṃ ca buddhiṃ ca vā sarvaṃ vā dehaprāṇabuddhi   
śūnyātmakaṃ (517) sarvaṃ vā tatraiva śivatāmayāṃ   
bhuvanakartṛtāyāṃ tāyāṃ nimajjayatyanavarataṃ tat tasmāt tāṃ   
bhuvanakartṛtāṃ vibhūti paryantāṃ labhate |  
  
	kathañcidāsādyetyādinā tadeva śivarūpameva cet tarhi tasya   
śivātmano vastunaḥ pratyabhijñānāpratyabhijñānayoraviśeṣaḥ bījaṃ   
pramātrā apratyabhijñātamapi salilādi sahakārisākalye kimaṃkuraṃ na   
janayati pramātrā apratyabhijñātamapyaṃkuraṃ janayatyeva |   
tadvadātmākhyaṃ vastvapratyabhijñātamapi śivarūpamevātmā īśvara   
iti pratyabhijñāne ko nibandhaḥ | apratyabhijñāne'pyātmā īśvara eva |
